3926   { PreserveReexecuteState preexecs(this);
3927     jvms()->set_should_reexecute(true);
3928 
3929     array_type_mirror = null_check(array_type_mirror);
3930     original          = null_check(original);
3931 
3932     // Check if a null path was taken unconditionally.
3933     if (stopped())  return true;
3934 
3935     Node* orig_length = load_array_length(original);
3936 
3937     Node* klass_node = load_klass_from_mirror(array_type_mirror, false, NULL, 0);
3938     klass_node = null_check(klass_node);
3939 
3940     RegionNode* bailout = new RegionNode(1);
3941     record_for_igvn(bailout);
3942 
3943     // Despite the generic type of Arrays.copyOf, the mirror might be int, int[], etc.
3944     // Bail out if that is so.
3945     // Value type array may have object field that would require a
3946     // write barrier. Conservatively, go to slow path.
3947     BarrierSetC2* bs = BarrierSet::barrier_set()->barrier_set_c2();
3948     Node* not_objArray = !bs->array_copy_requires_gc_barriers(false, T_OBJECT, false, BarrierSetC2::Parsing) ?
3949         generate_typeArray_guard(klass_node, bailout) : generate_non_objArray_guard(klass_node, bailout);
3950     if (not_objArray != NULL) {
3951       // Improve the klass node's type from the new optimistic assumption:
3952       ciKlass* ak = ciArrayKlass::make(env()->Object_klass());
3953       const Type* akls = TypeKlassPtr::make(TypePtr::NotNull, ak, Type::Offset(0), false);
3954       Node* cast = new CastPPNode(klass_node, akls);
3955       cast->init_req(0, control());
3956       klass_node = _gvn.transform(cast);
3957     }
3958 
3959     Node* original_kls = load_object_klass(original);
3960     // ArrayCopyNode:Ideal may transform the ArrayCopyNode to
3961     // loads/stores but it is legal only if we're sure the
3962     // Arrays.copyOf would succeed. So we need all input arguments
3963     // to the copyOf to be validated, including that the copy to the
3964     // new array won't trigger an ArrayStoreException. That subtype
3965     // check can be optimized if we know something on the type of
3966     // the input array from type speculation.
3967     if (_gvn.type(klass_node)->singleton() && !stopped()) {
3968       ciKlass* subk   = _gvn.type(original_kls)->is_klassptr()->klass();
3969       ciKlass* superk = _gvn.type(klass_node)->is_klassptr()->klass();
3970 
3971       int test = C->static_subtype_check(superk, subk);
3972       if (test != Compile::SSC_always_true && test != Compile::SSC_always_false) {
3973         const TypeOopPtr* t_original = _gvn.type(original)->is_oopptr();
3974         if (t_original->speculative_type() != NULL) {
3975           original = maybe_cast_profiled_obj(original, t_original->speculative_type(), true);
3976           original_kls = load_object_klass(original);
3977         }
3978       }
3979     }
3980 
3981     if (ValueArrayFlatten) {
3982       // Either both or neither new array klass and original array
3983       // klass must be flattened
3984       Node* is_flat = generate_valueArray_guard(klass_node, NULL);
3985       if (!original_t->is_not_flat()) {
3986         generate_valueArray_guard(original_kls, bailout);
3987       }
3988       if (is_flat != NULL) {
3989         RegionNode* r = new RegionNode(2);
3990         record_for_igvn(r);
3991         r->init_req(1, control());
3992         set_control(is_flat);
3993         if (!original_t->is_not_flat()) {
3994           generate_valueArray_guard(original_kls, r);
3995         }
3996         bailout->add_req(control());
3997         set_control(_gvn.transform(r));
3998       }
3999     }
4000 
4001     // Bail out if either start or end is negative.
4002     generate_negative_guard(start, bailout, &start);
4003     generate_negative_guard(end,   bailout, &end);
4004 
4005     Node* length = end;
4006     if (_gvn.type(start) != TypeInt::ZERO) {
4007       length = _gvn.transform(new SubINode(end, start));
4008     }
4009 
4010     // Bail out if length is negative.
4011     // Without this the new_array would throw
4012     // NegativeArraySizeException but IllegalArgumentException is what
4013     // should be thrown
4014     generate_negative_guard(length, bailout, &length);
4015 
4016     if (bailout->req() > 1) {
4017       PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
4018       set_control(_gvn.transform(bailout));
4019       uncommon_trap(Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic,
4020                     Deoptimization::Action_maybe_recompile);
4021     }
4022 
4023     if (!stopped()) {
4024       // How many elements will we copy from the original?
4025       // The answer is MinI(orig_length - start, length).
4026       Node* orig_tail = _gvn.transform(new SubINode(orig_length, start));
4027       Node* moved = generate_min_max(vmIntrinsics::_min, orig_tail, length);
4028 
4029       // Generate a direct call to the right arraycopy function(s).
4030       // We know the copy is disjoint but we might not know if the
4031       // oop stores need checking.
4032       // Extreme case:  Arrays.copyOf((Integer[])x, 10, String[].class).
4033       // This will fail a store-check if x contains any non-nulls.
4034 
4035       bool validated = false;
4036       // Reason_class_check rather than Reason_intrinsic because we
4037       // want to intrinsify even if this traps.
4038       if (!too_many_traps(Deoptimization::Reason_class_check)) {
4039         Node* not_subtype_ctrl = gen_subtype_check(original, klass_node);
4040 
4041         if (not_subtype_ctrl != top()) {
4042           PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
4043           set_control(not_subtype_ctrl);
4044           uncommon_trap(Deoptimization::Reason_class_check,
4045                         Deoptimization::Action_make_not_entrant);
4046           assert(stopped(), "Should be stopped");
4047         }
4048         validated = true;
4049       }
4050 
4051       if (!stopped()) {
4052         // Load element mirror
4053         Node* p = basic_plus_adr(array_type_mirror, java_lang_Class::component_mirror_offset_in_bytes());
4054         Node* elem_mirror = access_load_at(array_type_mirror, p, _gvn.type(p)->is_ptr(), TypeInstPtr::MIRROR, T_OBJECT, IN_HEAP);
4055 
4056         newcopy = new_array(klass_node, length, 0, NULL, false, elem_mirror);
4057 
4058         ArrayCopyNode* ac = ArrayCopyNode::make(this, true, original, start, newcopy, intcon(0), moved, true, false,
4059                                                 original_kls, klass_node);
4060         if (!is_copyOfRange) {
4061           ac->set_copyof(validated);
4062         } else {
4063           ac->set_copyofrange(validated);
4064         }
4065         Node* n = _gvn.transform(ac);
4066         if (n == ac) {
4067           ac->connect_outputs(this);
4068         } else {
4069           assert(validated, "shouldn't transform if all arguments not validated");
4070           set_all_memory(n);
4071         }
4072       }
4073     }
4074   } // original reexecute is set back here
4075 
4076   C->set_has_split_ifs(true); // Has chance for split-if optimization
4077   if (!stopped()) {
4078     set_result(newcopy);
4079   }
4080   return true;
4081 }
4082 
4083 
4084 //----------------------generate_virtual_guard---------------------------
4085 // Helper for hashCode and clone.  Peeks inside the vtable to avoid a call.
4086 Node* LibraryCallKit::generate_virtual_guard(Node* obj_klass,
4087                                              RegionNode* slow_region) {
4088   ciMethod* method = callee();
4089   int vtable_index = method->vtable_index();
4090   assert(vtable_index >= 0 || vtable_index == Method::nonvirtual_vtable_index,
4091          "bad index %d", vtable_index);
4092   // Get the Method* out of the appropriate vtable entry.
4093   int entry_offset  = in_bytes(Klass::vtable_start_offset()) +
4094                      vtable_index*vtableEntry::size_in_bytes() +
4095                      vtableEntry::method_offset_in_bytes();
4096   Node* entry_addr  = basic_plus_adr(obj_klass, entry_offset);
4097   Node* target_call = make_load(NULL, entry_addr, TypePtr::NOTNULL, T_ADDRESS, MemNode::unordered);
4098 
4099   // Compare the target method with the expected method (e.g., Object.hashCode).
4100   const TypePtr* native_call_addr = TypeMetadataPtr::make(method);
4101 
4102   Node* native_call = makecon(native_call_addr);
4103   Node* chk_native  = _gvn.transform(new CmpPNode(target_call, native_call));
4104   Node* test_native = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(chk_native, BoolTest::ne));
4105 
4106   return generate_slow_guard(test_native, slow_region);
4107 }
4108 
4109 //-----------------------generate_method_call----------------------------
4110 // Use generate_method_call to make a slow-call to the real
4111 // method if the fast path fails.  An alternative would be to
4112 // use a stub like OptoRuntime::slow_arraycopy_Java.
4113 // This only works for expanding the current library call,
4114 // not another intrinsic.  (E.g., don't use this for making an
4115 // arraycopy call inside of the copyOf intrinsic.)
4116 CallJavaNode*
4117 LibraryCallKit::generate_method_call(vmIntrinsics::ID method_id, bool is_virtual, bool is_static) {
4118   // When compiling the intrinsic method itself, do not use this technique.
4119   guarantee(callee() != C->method(), "cannot make slow-call to self");
4120 
4121   ciMethod* method = callee();
4122   // ensure the JVMS we have will be correct for this call
4123   guarantee(method_id == method->intrinsic_id(), "must match");
4124 
4125   const TypeFunc* tf = TypeFunc::make(method);
4126   CallJavaNode* slow_call;
4127   if (is_static) {
4128     assert(!is_virtual, "");
4129     slow_call = new CallStaticJavaNode(C, tf,
4130                            SharedRuntime::get_resolve_static_call_stub(),
4131                            method, bci());
4132   } else if (is_virtual) {
4133     null_check_receiver();
4134     int vtable_index = Method::invalid_vtable_index;
4135     if (UseInlineCaches) {
4136       // Suppress the vtable call
4137     } else {
4138       // hashCode and clone are not a miranda methods,
4139       // so the vtable index is fixed.
4140       // No need to use the linkResolver to get it.
4141        vtable_index = method->vtable_index();
4142        assert(vtable_index >= 0 || vtable_index == Method::nonvirtual_vtable_index,
4143               "bad index %d", vtable_index);
4144     }
4145     slow_call = new CallDynamicJavaNode(tf,
4146                           SharedRuntime::get_resolve_virtual_call_stub(),
4147                           method, vtable_index, bci());
4148   } else {  // neither virtual nor static:  opt_virtual
4149     null_check_receiver();
4150     slow_call = new CallStaticJavaNode(C, tf,
4151                                 SharedRuntime::get_resolve_opt_virtual_call_stub(),
4152                                 method, bci());
4153     slow_call->set_optimized_virtual(true);
4154   }
4155   if (CallGenerator::is_inlined_method_handle_intrinsic(this->method(), bci(), callee())) {
4156     // To be able to issue a direct call (optimized virtual or virtual)
4157     // and skip a call to MH.linkTo*/invokeBasic adapter, additional information
4158     // about the method being invoked should be attached to the call site to
4159     // make resolution logic work (see SharedRuntime::resolve_{virtual,opt_virtual}_call_C).
4160     slow_call->set_override_symbolic_info(true);
4161   }
4162   set_arguments_for_java_call(slow_call);
4163   set_edges_for_java_call(slow_call);
4164   return slow_call;
4165 }
4166 
4167 
4168 /**
4169  * Build special case code for calls to hashCode on an object. This call may
4170  * be virtual (invokevirtual) or bound (invokespecial). For each case we generate
4171  * slightly different code.
4172  */
4173 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_native_hashcode(bool is_virtual, bool is_static) {
4174   assert(is_static == callee()->is_static(), "correct intrinsic selection");
4175   assert(!(is_virtual && is_static), "either virtual, special, or static");
4176 
4177   enum { _slow_path = 1, _fast_path, _null_path, PATH_LIMIT };
4178 
4179   RegionNode* result_reg = new RegionNode(PATH_LIMIT);
4180   PhiNode*    result_val = new PhiNode(result_reg, TypeInt::INT);
4181   PhiNode*    result_io  = new PhiNode(result_reg, Type::ABIO);
4182   PhiNode*    result_mem = new PhiNode(result_reg, Type::MEMORY, TypePtr::BOTTOM);
4183   Node* obj = argument(0);
4184 
4185   if (obj->is_ValueType() || gvn().type(obj)->is_valuetypeptr()) {
4186     return false;
4187   }
4188 
4189   if (!is_static) {
4190     // Check for hashing null object
4191     obj = null_check_receiver();
4192     if (stopped())  return true;        // unconditionally null
4193     result_reg->init_req(_null_path, top());
4194     result_val->init_req(_null_path, top());
4195   } else {
4196     // Do a null check, and return zero if null.
4197     // System.identityHashCode(null) == 0
4198     Node* null_ctl = top();
4199     obj = null_check_oop(obj, &null_ctl);
4200     result_reg->init_req(_null_path, null_ctl);
4201     result_val->init_req(_null_path, _gvn.intcon(0));
4202   }
4203 
4204   // Unconditionally null?  Then return right away.
4205   if (stopped()) {
4206     set_control( result_reg->in(_null_path));
4207     if (!stopped())
4208       set_result(result_val->in(_null_path));
4209     return true;
4210   }
4211 
4212   // We only go to the fast case code if we pass a number of guards.  The
4213   // paths which do not pass are accumulated in the slow_region.
4214   RegionNode* slow_region = new RegionNode(1);
4215   record_for_igvn(slow_region);
4216 
4217   // If this is a virtual call, we generate a funny guard.  We pull out
4218   // the vtable entry corresponding to hashCode() from the target object.
4219   // If the target method which we are calling happens to be the native
4220   // Object hashCode() method, we pass the guard.  We do not need this
4221   // guard for non-virtual calls -- the caller is known to be the native
4222   // Object hashCode().
4223   if (is_virtual) {
4224     // After null check, get the object's klass.
4225     Node* obj_klass = load_object_klass(obj);
4226     generate_virtual_guard(obj_klass, slow_region);
4227   }
4228 
4229   // Get the header out of the object, use LoadMarkNode when available
4230   Node* header_addr = basic_plus_adr(obj, oopDesc::mark_offset_in_bytes());
4231   // The control of the load must be NULL. Otherwise, the load can move before
4232   // the null check after castPP removal.
4233   Node* no_ctrl = NULL;
4234   Node* header = make_load(no_ctrl, header_addr, TypeX_X, TypeX_X->basic_type(), MemNode::unordered);
4235 
4236   // Test the header to see if it is unlocked.
4237   // This also serves as guard against value types (they have the always_locked_pattern set).
4238   Node *lock_mask      = _gvn.MakeConX(markWord::biased_lock_mask_in_place);
4239   Node *lmasked_header = _gvn.transform(new AndXNode(header, lock_mask));
4240   Node *unlocked_val   = _gvn.MakeConX(markWord::unlocked_value);
4241   Node *chk_unlocked   = _gvn.transform(new CmpXNode( lmasked_header, unlocked_val));
4242   Node *test_unlocked  = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode( chk_unlocked, BoolTest::ne));
4243 
4244   generate_slow_guard(test_unlocked, slow_region);
4245 
4246   // Get the hash value and check to see that it has been properly assigned.
4247   // We depend on hash_mask being at most 32 bits and avoid the use of
4248   // hash_mask_in_place because it could be larger than 32 bits in a 64-bit
4249   // vm: see markWord.hpp.
4250   Node *hash_mask      = _gvn.intcon(markWord::hash_mask);
4251   Node *hash_shift     = _gvn.intcon(markWord::hash_shift);
4252   Node *hshifted_header= _gvn.transform(new URShiftXNode(header, hash_shift));
4253   // This hack lets the hash bits live anywhere in the mark object now, as long
4254   // as the shift drops the relevant bits into the low 32 bits.  Note that
4255   // Java spec says that HashCode is an int so there's no point in capturing
4256   // an 'X'-sized hashcode (32 in 32-bit build or 64 in 64-bit build).
4257   hshifted_header      = ConvX2I(hshifted_header);
4258   Node *hash_val       = _gvn.transform(new AndINode(hshifted_header, hash_mask));
4259 
4260   Node *no_hash_val    = _gvn.intcon(markWord::no_hash);
4261   Node *chk_assigned   = _gvn.transform(new CmpINode( hash_val, no_hash_val));
4262   Node *test_assigned  = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode( chk_assigned, BoolTest::eq));
4263 
4264   generate_slow_guard(test_assigned, slow_region);
4265 
4266   Node* init_mem = reset_memory();
4267   // fill in the rest of the null path:
4268   result_io ->init_req(_null_path, i_o());
4269   result_mem->init_req(_null_path, init_mem);
4270 
4271   result_val->init_req(_fast_path, hash_val);
4272   result_reg->init_req(_fast_path, control());
4273   result_io ->init_req(_fast_path, i_o());
4274   result_mem->init_req(_fast_path, init_mem);
4275 
4276   // Generate code for the slow case.  We make a call to hashCode().
4277   set_control(_gvn.transform(slow_region));
4278   if (!stopped()) {
4279     // No need for PreserveJVMState, because we're using up the present state.
4280     set_all_memory(init_mem);
4281     vmIntrinsics::ID hashCode_id = is_static ? vmIntrinsics::_identityHashCode : vmIntrinsics::_hashCode;
4282     CallJavaNode* slow_call = generate_method_call(hashCode_id, is_virtual, is_static);
4283     Node* slow_result = set_results_for_java_call(slow_call);
4284     // this->control() comes from set_results_for_java_call
4285     result_reg->init_req(_slow_path, control());
4286     result_val->init_req(_slow_path, slow_result);
4287     result_io  ->set_req(_slow_path, i_o());
4288     result_mem ->set_req(_slow_path, reset_memory());
4289   }
4290 
4291   // Return the combined state.
4292   set_i_o(        _gvn.transform(result_io)  );
4293   set_all_memory( _gvn.transform(result_mem));
4294 
4295   set_result(result_reg, result_val);
4296   return true;
4297 }
4298 
4299 //---------------------------inline_native_getClass----------------------------
4300 // public final native Class<?> java.lang.Object.getClass();
4301 //
4302 // Build special case code for calls to getClass on an object.
4303 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_native_getClass() {
4304   Node* obj = argument(0);
4305   if (obj->is_ValueType()) {
4306     ciKlass* vk = _gvn.type(obj)->value_klass();
4307     set_result(makecon(TypeInstPtr::make(vk->java_mirror())));
4308     return true;
4309   }
4310   obj = null_check_receiver();
4311   if (stopped())  return true;
4312   set_result(load_mirror_from_klass(load_object_klass(obj)));
4313   return true;
4314 }
4315 
4316 //-----------------inline_native_Reflection_getCallerClass---------------------
4317 // public static native Class<?> sun.reflect.Reflection.getCallerClass();
4318 //
4319 // In the presence of deep enough inlining, getCallerClass() becomes a no-op.
4320 //
4321 // NOTE: This code must perform the same logic as JVM_GetCallerClass
4322 // in that it must skip particular security frames and checks for
4323 // caller sensitive methods.
4324 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_native_Reflection_getCallerClass() {
4325 #ifndef PRODUCT
4326   if ((C->print_intrinsics() || C->print_inlining()) && Verbose) {
4327     tty->print_cr("Attempting to inline sun.reflect.Reflection.getCallerClass");
4328   }
4329 #endif
4330 
4331   if (!jvms()->has_method()) {
4332 #ifndef PRODUCT
4333     if ((C->print_intrinsics() || C->print_inlining()) && Verbose) {
4334       tty->print_cr("  Bailing out because intrinsic was inlined at top level");
4335     }
4336 #endif
4337     return false;
4338   }
4339 
4340   // Walk back up the JVM state to find the caller at the required
4341   // depth.
4342   JVMState* caller_jvms = jvms();
4343 
4344   // Cf. JVM_GetCallerClass
4345   // NOTE: Start the loop at depth 1 because the current JVM state does
4346   // not include the Reflection.getCallerClass() frame.
4347   for (int n = 1; caller_jvms != NULL; caller_jvms = caller_jvms->caller(), n++) {
4348     ciMethod* m = caller_jvms->method();
4349     switch (n) {
4350     case 0:
4351       fatal("current JVM state does not include the Reflection.getCallerClass frame");
4352       break;
4353     case 1:
4354       // Frame 0 and 1 must be caller sensitive (see JVM_GetCallerClass).
4355       if (!m->caller_sensitive()) {
4356 #ifndef PRODUCT
4357         if ((C->print_intrinsics() || C->print_inlining()) && Verbose) {
4358           tty->print_cr("  Bailing out: CallerSensitive annotation expected at frame %d", n);
4359         }
4360 #endif
4361         return false;  // bail-out; let JVM_GetCallerClass do the work
4362       }
4363       break;
4364     default:
4365       if (!m->is_ignored_by_security_stack_walk()) {
4366         // We have reached the desired frame; return the holder class.
4367         // Acquire method holder as java.lang.Class and push as constant.
4368         ciInstanceKlass* caller_klass = caller_jvms->method()->holder();
4369         ciInstance* caller_mirror = caller_klass->java_mirror();
4370         set_result(makecon(TypeInstPtr::make(caller_mirror)));
4371 
4372 #ifndef PRODUCT
4373         if ((C->print_intrinsics() || C->print_inlining()) && Verbose) {
4374           tty->print_cr("  Succeeded: caller = %d) %s.%s, JVMS depth = %d", n, caller_klass->name()->as_utf8(), caller_jvms->method()->name()->as_utf8(), jvms()->depth());
4375           tty->print_cr("  JVM state at this point:");
4376           for (int i = jvms()->depth(), n = 1; i >= 1; i--, n++) {
4377             ciMethod* m = jvms()->of_depth(i)->method();
4378             tty->print_cr("   %d) %s.%s", n, m->holder()->name()->as_utf8(), m->name()->as_utf8());
4379           }
4380         }
4381 #endif
4382         return true;
4383       }
4384       break;
4385     }
4386   }
4387 
4388 #ifndef PRODUCT
4389   if ((C->print_intrinsics() || C->print_inlining()) && Verbose) {
4390     tty->print_cr("  Bailing out because caller depth exceeded inlining depth = %d", jvms()->depth());
4391     tty->print_cr("  JVM state at this point:");
4392     for (int i = jvms()->depth(), n = 1; i >= 1; i--, n++) {
4393       ciMethod* m = jvms()->of_depth(i)->method();
4394       tty->print_cr("   %d) %s.%s", n, m->holder()->name()->as_utf8(), m->name()->as_utf8());
4395     }
4396   }
4397 #endif
4398 
4399   return false;  // bail-out; let JVM_GetCallerClass do the work
4400 }
4401 
4402 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_fp_conversions(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
4403   Node* arg = argument(0);
4404   Node* result = NULL;
4405 
4406   switch (id) {
4407   case vmIntrinsics::_floatToRawIntBits:    result = new MoveF2INode(arg);  break;
4408   case vmIntrinsics::_intBitsToFloat:       result = new MoveI2FNode(arg);  break;
4409   case vmIntrinsics::_doubleToRawLongBits:  result = new MoveD2LNode(arg);  break;
4410   case vmIntrinsics::_longBitsToDouble:     result = new MoveL2DNode(arg);  break;
4411 
4412   case vmIntrinsics::_doubleToLongBits: {
4413     // two paths (plus control) merge in a wood
4414     RegionNode *r = new RegionNode(3);
4415     Node *phi = new PhiNode(r, TypeLong::LONG);
4416 
4417     Node *cmpisnan = _gvn.transform(new CmpDNode(arg, arg));
4418     // Build the boolean node
4419     Node *bolisnan = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmpisnan, BoolTest::ne));
4420 
4421     // Branch either way.
4422     // NaN case is less traveled, which makes all the difference.
4423     IfNode *ifisnan = create_and_xform_if(control(), bolisnan, PROB_STATIC_FREQUENT, COUNT_UNKNOWN);
4424     Node *opt_isnan = _gvn.transform(ifisnan);
4425     assert( opt_isnan->is_If(), "Expect an IfNode");
4426     IfNode *opt_ifisnan = (IfNode*)opt_isnan;
4427     Node *iftrue = _gvn.transform(new IfTrueNode(opt_ifisnan));
4428 
4429     set_control(iftrue);
4430 
4431     static const jlong nan_bits = CONST64(0x7ff8000000000000);
4432     Node *slow_result = longcon(nan_bits); // return NaN
4433     phi->init_req(1, _gvn.transform( slow_result ));
4434     r->init_req(1, iftrue);
4435 
4436     // Else fall through
4437     Node *iffalse = _gvn.transform(new IfFalseNode(opt_ifisnan));
4438     set_control(iffalse);
4439 
4440     phi->init_req(2, _gvn.transform(new MoveD2LNode(arg)));
4441     r->init_req(2, iffalse);
4442 
4443     // Post merge
4444     set_control(_gvn.transform(r));
4445     record_for_igvn(r);
4446 
4447     C->set_has_split_ifs(true); // Has chance for split-if optimization
4448     result = phi;
4449     assert(result->bottom_type()->isa_long(), "must be");
4450     break;
4451   }
4452 
4453   case vmIntrinsics::_floatToIntBits: {
4454     // two paths (plus control) merge in a wood
4455     RegionNode *r = new RegionNode(3);
4456     Node *phi = new PhiNode(r, TypeInt::INT);
4457 
4458     Node *cmpisnan = _gvn.transform(new CmpFNode(arg, arg));
4459     // Build the boolean node
4460     Node *bolisnan = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmpisnan, BoolTest::ne));
4461 
4462     // Branch either way.
4463     // NaN case is less traveled, which makes all the difference.
4464     IfNode *ifisnan = create_and_xform_if(control(), bolisnan, PROB_STATIC_FREQUENT, COUNT_UNKNOWN);
4465     Node *opt_isnan = _gvn.transform(ifisnan);
4466     assert( opt_isnan->is_If(), "Expect an IfNode");
4467     IfNode *opt_ifisnan = (IfNode*)opt_isnan;
4468     Node *iftrue = _gvn.transform(new IfTrueNode(opt_ifisnan));
4469 
4470     set_control(iftrue);
4471 
4472     static const jint nan_bits = 0x7fc00000;
4473     Node *slow_result = makecon(TypeInt::make(nan_bits)); // return NaN
4474     phi->init_req(1, _gvn.transform( slow_result ));
4475     r->init_req(1, iftrue);
4476 
4477     // Else fall through
4478     Node *iffalse = _gvn.transform(new IfFalseNode(opt_ifisnan));
4479     set_control(iffalse);
4480 
4481     phi->init_req(2, _gvn.transform(new MoveF2INode(arg)));
4482     r->init_req(2, iffalse);
4483 
4484     // Post merge
4485     set_control(_gvn.transform(r));
4486     record_for_igvn(r);
4487 
4488     C->set_has_split_ifs(true); // Has chance for split-if optimization
4489     result = phi;
4490     assert(result->bottom_type()->isa_int(), "must be");
4491     break;
4492   }
4493 
4494   default:
4495     fatal_unexpected_iid(id);
4496     break;
4497   }
4498   set_result(_gvn.transform(result));
4499   return true;
4500 }
4501 
4502 //----------------------inline_unsafe_copyMemory-------------------------
4503 // public native void Unsafe.copyMemory0(Object srcBase, long srcOffset, Object destBase, long destOffset, long bytes);
4504 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_unsafe_copyMemory() {
4505   if (callee()->is_static())  return false;  // caller must have the capability!
4506   null_check_receiver();  // null-check receiver
4507   if (stopped())  return true;
4508 
4509   C->set_has_unsafe_access(true);  // Mark eventual nmethod as "unsafe".
4510 
4511   Node* src_ptr =         argument(1);   // type: oop
4512   Node* src_off = ConvL2X(argument(2));  // type: long
4513   Node* dst_ptr =         argument(4);   // type: oop
4514   Node* dst_off = ConvL2X(argument(5));  // type: long
4515   Node* size    = ConvL2X(argument(7));  // type: long
4516 
4517   assert(Unsafe_field_offset_to_byte_offset(11) == 11,
4518          "fieldOffset must be byte-scaled");
4519 
4520   Node* src = make_unsafe_address(src_ptr, src_off, ACCESS_READ);
4521   Node* dst = make_unsafe_address(dst_ptr, dst_off, ACCESS_WRITE);
4522 
4523   // Conservatively insert a memory barrier on all memory slices.
4524   // Do not let writes of the copy source or destination float below the copy.
4525   insert_mem_bar(Op_MemBarCPUOrder);
4526 
4527   Node* thread = _gvn.transform(new ThreadLocalNode());
4528   Node* doing_unsafe_access_addr = basic_plus_adr(top(), thread, in_bytes(JavaThread::doing_unsafe_access_offset()));
4529   BasicType doing_unsafe_access_bt = T_BYTE;
4530   assert((sizeof(bool) * CHAR_BIT) == 8, "not implemented");
4531 
4532   // update volatile field
4533   store_to_memory(control(), doing_unsafe_access_addr, intcon(1), doing_unsafe_access_bt, Compile::AliasIdxRaw, MemNode::unordered);
4534 
4535   // Call it.  Note that the length argument is not scaled.
4536   make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
4537                     OptoRuntime::fast_arraycopy_Type(),
4538                     StubRoutines::unsafe_arraycopy(),
4539                     "unsafe_arraycopy",
4540                     TypeRawPtr::BOTTOM,
4541                     src, dst, size XTOP);
4542 
4543   store_to_memory(control(), doing_unsafe_access_addr, intcon(0), doing_unsafe_access_bt, Compile::AliasIdxRaw, MemNode::unordered);
4544 
4545   // Do not let reads of the copy destination float above the copy.
4546   insert_mem_bar(Op_MemBarCPUOrder);
4547 
4548   return true;
4549 }
4550 
4551 //------------------------clone_coping-----------------------------------
4552 // Helper function for inline_native_clone.
4553 void LibraryCallKit::copy_to_clone(Node* obj, Node* alloc_obj, Node* obj_size, bool is_array) {
4554   assert(obj_size != NULL, "");
4555   Node* raw_obj = alloc_obj->in(1);
4556   assert(alloc_obj->is_CheckCastPP() && raw_obj->is_Proj() && raw_obj->in(0)->is_Allocate(), "");
4557 
4558   AllocateNode* alloc = NULL;
4559   if (ReduceBulkZeroing) {
4560     // We will be completely responsible for initializing this object -
4561     // mark Initialize node as complete.
4562     alloc = AllocateNode::Ideal_allocation(alloc_obj, &_gvn);
4563     // The object was just allocated - there should be no any stores!
4564     guarantee(alloc != NULL && alloc->maybe_set_complete(&_gvn), "");
4565     // Mark as complete_with_arraycopy so that on AllocateNode
4566     // expansion, we know this AllocateNode is initialized by an array
4567     // copy and a StoreStore barrier exists after the array copy.
4568     alloc->initialization()->set_complete_with_arraycopy();
4569   }
4570 
4571   Node* size = _gvn.transform(obj_size);
4572   // Exclude the header but include array length to copy by 8 bytes words.
4573   // Can't use base_offset_in_bytes(bt) since basic type is unknown.
4574   int base_off = BarrierSetC2::arraycopy_payload_base_offset(is_array);
4575   Node* countx = size;
4576   countx = _gvn.transform(new SubXNode(countx, MakeConX(base_off)));
4577   countx = _gvn.transform(new URShiftXNode(countx, intcon(LogBytesPerLong)));
4578 
4579   access_clone(obj, alloc_obj, countx, is_array);
4580 
4581   // Do not let reads from the cloned object float above the arraycopy.
4582   if (alloc != NULL) {
4583     // Do not let stores that initialize this object be reordered with
4584     // a subsequent store that would make this object accessible by
4585     // other threads.
4586     // Record what AllocateNode this StoreStore protects so that
4587     // escape analysis can go from the MemBarStoreStoreNode to the
4588     // AllocateNode and eliminate the MemBarStoreStoreNode if possible
4589     // based on the escape status of the AllocateNode.
4590     insert_mem_bar(Op_MemBarStoreStore, alloc->proj_out_or_null(AllocateNode::RawAddress));
4591   } else {
4592     insert_mem_bar(Op_MemBarCPUOrder);
4593   }
4594 }
4595 
4596 //------------------------inline_native_clone----------------------------
4597 // protected native Object java.lang.Object.clone();
4598 //
4599 // Here are the simple edge cases:
4600 //  null receiver => normal trap
4601 //  virtual and clone was overridden => slow path to out-of-line clone
4602 //  not cloneable or finalizer => slow path to out-of-line Object.clone
4603 //
4604 // The general case has two steps, allocation and copying.
4605 // Allocation has two cases, and uses GraphKit::new_instance or new_array.
4606 //
4607 // Copying also has two cases, oop arrays and everything else.
4608 // Oop arrays use arrayof_oop_arraycopy (same as System.arraycopy).
4609 // Everything else uses the tight inline loop supplied by CopyArrayNode.
4610 //
4611 // These steps fold up nicely if and when the cloned object's klass
4612 // can be sharply typed as an object array, a type array, or an instance.
4613 //
4614 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_native_clone(bool is_virtual) {
4615   PhiNode* result_val;
4616 
4617   // Set the reexecute bit for the interpreter to reexecute
4618   // the bytecode that invokes Object.clone if deoptimization happens.
4619   { PreserveReexecuteState preexecs(this);
4620     jvms()->set_should_reexecute(true);
4621 
4622     Node* obj = argument(0);
4623     if (obj->is_ValueType()) {
4624       return false;
4625     }
4626 
4627     obj = null_check_receiver();
4628     if (stopped())  return true;
4629 
4630     const TypeOopPtr* obj_type = _gvn.type(obj)->is_oopptr();
4631 
4632     // If we are going to clone an instance, we need its exact type to
4633     // know the number and types of fields to convert the clone to
4634     // loads/stores. Maybe a speculative type can help us.
4635     if (!obj_type->klass_is_exact() &&
4636         obj_type->speculative_type() != NULL &&
4637         obj_type->speculative_type()->is_instance_klass() &&
4638         !obj_type->speculative_type()->is_valuetype()) {
4639       ciInstanceKlass* spec_ik = obj_type->speculative_type()->as_instance_klass();
4640       if (spec_ik->nof_nonstatic_fields() <= ArrayCopyLoadStoreMaxElem &&
4641           !spec_ik->has_injected_fields()) {
4642         ciKlass* k = obj_type->klass();
4643         if (!k->is_instance_klass() ||
4644             k->as_instance_klass()->is_interface() ||
4645             k->as_instance_klass()->has_subklass()) {
4646           obj = maybe_cast_profiled_obj(obj, obj_type->speculative_type(), false);
4647         }
4648       }
4649     }
4650 
4651     // Conservatively insert a memory barrier on all memory slices.
4652     // Do not let writes into the original float below the clone.
4653     insert_mem_bar(Op_MemBarCPUOrder);
4654 
4655     // paths into result_reg:
4656     enum {
4657       _slow_path = 1,     // out-of-line call to clone method (virtual or not)
4658       _objArray_path,     // plain array allocation, plus arrayof_oop_arraycopy
4659       _array_path,        // plain array allocation, plus arrayof_long_arraycopy
4660       _instance_path,     // plain instance allocation, plus arrayof_long_arraycopy
4661       PATH_LIMIT
4662     };
4663     RegionNode* result_reg = new RegionNode(PATH_LIMIT);
4664     result_val             = new PhiNode(result_reg, TypeInstPtr::NOTNULL);
4665     PhiNode*    result_i_o = new PhiNode(result_reg, Type::ABIO);
4666     PhiNode*    result_mem = new PhiNode(result_reg, Type::MEMORY, TypePtr::BOTTOM);
4667     record_for_igvn(result_reg);
4668 
4669     Node* obj_klass = load_object_klass(obj);
4670     // We only go to the fast case code if we pass a number of guards.
4671     // The paths which do not pass are accumulated in the slow_region.
4672     RegionNode* slow_region = new RegionNode(1);
4673     record_for_igvn(slow_region);
4674 
4675     Node* array_ctl = generate_array_guard(obj_klass, (RegionNode*)NULL);
4676     if (array_ctl != NULL) {
4677       // It's an array.
4678       PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
4679       set_control(array_ctl);
4680 
4681       BarrierSetC2* bs = BarrierSet::barrier_set()->barrier_set_c2();
4682       if (bs->array_copy_requires_gc_barriers(true, T_OBJECT, true, BarrierSetC2::Parsing) &&
4683           (!obj_type->isa_aryptr() || !obj_type->is_aryptr()->is_not_flat())) {
4684         // Flattened value type array may have object field that would require a
4685         // write barrier. Conservatively, go to slow path.
4686         generate_valueArray_guard(obj_klass, slow_region);
4687       }
4688 
4689       if (!stopped()) {
4690         Node* obj_length = load_array_length(obj);
4691         Node* obj_size  = NULL;
4692         // Load element mirror
4693         Node* array_type_mirror = load_mirror_from_klass(obj_klass);
4694         Node* p = basic_plus_adr(array_type_mirror, java_lang_Class::component_mirror_offset_in_bytes());
4695         Node* elem_mirror = access_load_at(array_type_mirror, p, _gvn.type(p)->is_ptr(), TypeInstPtr::MIRROR, T_OBJECT, IN_HEAP);
4696 
4697         Node* alloc_obj = new_array(obj_klass, obj_length, 0, &obj_size, false, elem_mirror);
4698 
4699         BarrierSetC2* bs = BarrierSet::barrier_set()->barrier_set_c2();
4700         if (bs->array_copy_requires_gc_barriers(true, T_OBJECT, true, BarrierSetC2::Parsing)) {
4701           // If it is an oop array, it requires very special treatment,
4702           // because gc barriers are required when accessing the array.
4703           Node* is_obja = generate_objArray_guard(obj_klass, (RegionNode*)NULL);
4704           if (is_obja != NULL) {
4705             PreserveJVMState pjvms2(this);
4706             set_control(is_obja);
4707             // Generate a direct call to the right arraycopy function(s).
4708             Node* alloc = tightly_coupled_allocation(alloc_obj, NULL);
4709             ArrayCopyNode* ac = ArrayCopyNode::make(this, true, obj, intcon(0), alloc_obj, intcon(0), obj_length, alloc != NULL, false);
4710             ac->set_clone_oop_array();
4711             Node* n = _gvn.transform(ac);
4712             assert(n == ac, "cannot disappear");
4713             ac->connect_outputs(this);
4714 
4715             result_reg->init_req(_objArray_path, control());
4716             result_val->init_req(_objArray_path, alloc_obj);
4717             result_i_o ->set_req(_objArray_path, i_o());
4718             result_mem ->set_req(_objArray_path, reset_memory());
4719           }
4720         }
4721         // Otherwise, there are no barriers to worry about.
4722         // (We can dispense with card marks if we know the allocation
4723         //  comes out of eden (TLAB)...  In fact, ReduceInitialCardMarks
4724         //  causes the non-eden paths to take compensating steps to
4725         //  simulate a fresh allocation, so that no further
4726         //  card marks are required in compiled code to initialize
4727         //  the object.)
4728 
4729         if (!stopped()) {
4730           copy_to_clone(obj, alloc_obj, obj_size, true);
4731 
4732           // Present the results of the copy.
4733           result_reg->init_req(_array_path, control());
4734           result_val->init_req(_array_path, alloc_obj);
4735           result_i_o ->set_req(_array_path, i_o());
4736           result_mem ->set_req(_array_path, reset_memory());
4737         }
4738       }
4739     }
4740 
4741     if (!stopped()) {
4742       // It's an instance (we did array above).  Make the slow-path tests.
4743       // If this is a virtual call, we generate a funny guard.  We grab
4744       // the vtable entry corresponding to clone() from the target object.
4745       // If the target method which we are calling happens to be the
4746       // Object clone() method, we pass the guard.  We do not need this
4747       // guard for non-virtual calls; the caller is known to be the native
4748       // Object clone().
4749       if (is_virtual) {
4750         generate_virtual_guard(obj_klass, slow_region);
4751       }
4752 
4753       // The object must be easily cloneable and must not have a finalizer.
4754       // Both of these conditions may be checked in a single test.
4755       // We could optimize the test further, but we don't care.
4756       generate_access_flags_guard(obj_klass,
4757                                   // Test both conditions:
4758                                   JVM_ACC_IS_CLONEABLE_FAST | JVM_ACC_HAS_FINALIZER,
4759                                   // Must be cloneable but not finalizer:
4760                                   JVM_ACC_IS_CLONEABLE_FAST,
4761                                   slow_region);
4762     }
4763 
4764     if (!stopped()) {
4765       // It's an instance, and it passed the slow-path tests.
4766       PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
4767       Node* obj_size  = NULL;
4768       // Need to deoptimize on exception from allocation since Object.clone intrinsic
4769       // is reexecuted if deoptimization occurs and there could be problems when merging
4770       // exception state between multiple Object.clone versions (reexecute=true vs reexecute=false).
4771       Node* alloc_obj = new_instance(obj_klass, NULL, &obj_size, /*deoptimize_on_exception=*/true);
4772 
4773       copy_to_clone(obj, alloc_obj, obj_size, false);
4774 
4775       // Present the results of the slow call.
4776       result_reg->init_req(_instance_path, control());
4777       result_val->init_req(_instance_path, alloc_obj);
4778       result_i_o ->set_req(_instance_path, i_o());
4779       result_mem ->set_req(_instance_path, reset_memory());
4780     }
4781 
4782     // Generate code for the slow case.  We make a call to clone().
4783     set_control(_gvn.transform(slow_region));
4784     if (!stopped()) {
4785       PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
4786       CallJavaNode* slow_call = generate_method_call(vmIntrinsics::_clone, is_virtual);
4787       // We need to deoptimize on exception (see comment above)
4788       Node* slow_result = set_results_for_java_call(slow_call, false, /* deoptimize */ true);
4789       // this->control() comes from set_results_for_java_call
4790       result_reg->init_req(_slow_path, control());
4791       result_val->init_req(_slow_path, slow_result);
4792       result_i_o ->set_req(_slow_path, i_o());
4793       result_mem ->set_req(_slow_path, reset_memory());
4794     }
4795 
4796     // Return the combined state.
4797     set_control(    _gvn.transform(result_reg));
4798     set_i_o(        _gvn.transform(result_i_o));
4799     set_all_memory( _gvn.transform(result_mem));
4800   } // original reexecute is set back here
4801 
4802   set_result(_gvn.transform(result_val));
4803   return true;
4804 }
4805 
4806 // If we have a tightly coupled allocation, the arraycopy may take care
4807 // of the array initialization. If one of the guards we insert between
4808 // the allocation and the arraycopy causes a deoptimization, an
4809 // unitialized array will escape the compiled method. To prevent that
4810 // we set the JVM state for uncommon traps between the allocation and
4811 // the arraycopy to the state before the allocation so, in case of
4812 // deoptimization, we'll reexecute the allocation and the
4813 // initialization.
4814 JVMState* LibraryCallKit::arraycopy_restore_alloc_state(AllocateArrayNode* alloc, int& saved_reexecute_sp) {
4815   if (alloc != NULL) {
4816     ciMethod* trap_method = alloc->jvms()->method();
4817     int trap_bci = alloc->jvms()->bci();
4818 
4819     if (!C->too_many_traps(trap_method, trap_bci, Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic) &&
4820         !C->too_many_traps(trap_method, trap_bci, Deoptimization::Reason_null_check)) {
4821       // Make sure there's no store between the allocation and the
4822       // arraycopy otherwise visible side effects could be rexecuted
4823       // in case of deoptimization and cause incorrect execution.
4824       bool no_interfering_store = true;
4825       Node* mem = alloc->in(TypeFunc::Memory);
4826       if (mem->is_MergeMem()) {
4827         for (MergeMemStream mms(merged_memory(), mem->as_MergeMem()); mms.next_non_empty2(); ) {
4828           Node* n = mms.memory();
4829           if (n != mms.memory2() && !(n->is_Proj() && n->in(0) == alloc->initialization())) {
4830             assert(n->is_Store(), "what else?");
4831             no_interfering_store = false;
4832             break;
4833           }
4834         }
4835       } else {
4836         for (MergeMemStream mms(merged_memory()); mms.next_non_empty(); ) {
4837           Node* n = mms.memory();
4838           if (n != mem && !(n->is_Proj() && n->in(0) == alloc->initialization())) {
4839             assert(n->is_Store(), "what else?");
4840             no_interfering_store = false;
4841             break;
4842           }
4843         }
4844       }
4845 
4846       if (no_interfering_store) {
4847         JVMState* old_jvms = alloc->jvms()->clone_shallow(C);
4848         uint size = alloc->req();
4849         SafePointNode* sfpt = new SafePointNode(size, old_jvms);
4850         old_jvms->set_map(sfpt);
4851         for (uint i = 0; i < size; i++) {
4852           sfpt->init_req(i, alloc->in(i));
4853         }
4854         // re-push array length for deoptimization
4855         sfpt->ins_req(old_jvms->stkoff() + old_jvms->sp(), alloc->in(AllocateNode::ALength));
4856         old_jvms->set_sp(old_jvms->sp()+1);
4857         old_jvms->set_monoff(old_jvms->monoff()+1);
4858         old_jvms->set_scloff(old_jvms->scloff()+1);
4859         old_jvms->set_endoff(old_jvms->endoff()+1);
4860         old_jvms->set_should_reexecute(true);
4861 
4862         sfpt->set_i_o(map()->i_o());
4863         sfpt->set_memory(map()->memory());
4864         sfpt->set_control(map()->control());
4865 
4866         JVMState* saved_jvms = jvms();
4867         saved_reexecute_sp = _reexecute_sp;
4868 
4869         set_jvms(sfpt->jvms());
4870         _reexecute_sp = jvms()->sp();
4871 
4872         return saved_jvms;
4873       }
4874     }
4875   }
4876   return NULL;
4877 }
4878 
4879 // In case of a deoptimization, we restart execution at the
4880 // allocation, allocating a new array. We would leave an uninitialized
4881 // array in the heap that GCs wouldn't expect. Move the allocation
4882 // after the traps so we don't allocate the array if we
4883 // deoptimize. This is possible because tightly_coupled_allocation()
4884 // guarantees there's no observer of the allocated array at this point
4885 // and the control flow is simple enough.
4886 void LibraryCallKit::arraycopy_move_allocation_here(AllocateArrayNode* alloc, Node* dest, JVMState* saved_jvms,
4887                                                     int saved_reexecute_sp, uint new_idx) {
4888   if (saved_jvms != NULL && !stopped()) {
4889     assert(alloc != NULL, "only with a tightly coupled allocation");
4890     // restore JVM state to the state at the arraycopy
4891     saved_jvms->map()->set_control(map()->control());
4892     assert(saved_jvms->map()->memory() == map()->memory(), "memory state changed?");
4893     assert(saved_jvms->map()->i_o() == map()->i_o(), "IO state changed?");
4894     // If we've improved the types of some nodes (null check) while
4895     // emitting the guards, propagate them to the current state
4896     map()->replaced_nodes().apply(saved_jvms->map(), new_idx);
4897     set_jvms(saved_jvms);
4898     _reexecute_sp = saved_reexecute_sp;
4899 
4900     // Remove the allocation from above the guards
4901     CallProjections* callprojs = alloc->extract_projections(true);
4902     InitializeNode* init = alloc->initialization();
4903     Node* alloc_mem = alloc->in(TypeFunc::Memory);
4904     C->gvn_replace_by(callprojs->fallthrough_ioproj, alloc->in(TypeFunc::I_O));
4905     C->gvn_replace_by(init->proj_out(TypeFunc::Memory), alloc_mem);
4906     C->gvn_replace_by(init->proj_out(TypeFunc::Control), alloc->in(0));
4907 
4908     // move the allocation here (after the guards)
4909     _gvn.hash_delete(alloc);
4910     alloc->set_req(TypeFunc::Control, control());
4911     alloc->set_req(TypeFunc::I_O, i_o());
4912     Node *mem = reset_memory();
4913     set_all_memory(mem);
4914     alloc->set_req(TypeFunc::Memory, mem);
4915     set_control(init->proj_out_or_null(TypeFunc::Control));
4916     set_i_o(callprojs->fallthrough_ioproj);
4917 
4918     // Update memory as done in GraphKit::set_output_for_allocation()
4919     const TypeInt* length_type = _gvn.find_int_type(alloc->in(AllocateNode::ALength));
4920     const TypeOopPtr* ary_type = _gvn.type(alloc->in(AllocateNode::KlassNode))->is_klassptr()->as_instance_type();
4921     if (ary_type->isa_aryptr() && length_type != NULL) {
4922       ary_type = ary_type->is_aryptr()->cast_to_size(length_type);
4923     }
4924     const TypePtr* telemref = ary_type->add_offset(Type::OffsetBot);
4925     int            elemidx  = C->get_alias_index(telemref);
4926     set_memory(init->proj_out_or_null(TypeFunc::Memory), Compile::AliasIdxRaw);
4927     set_memory(init->proj_out_or_null(TypeFunc::Memory), elemidx);
4928 
4929     Node* allocx = _gvn.transform(alloc);
4930     assert(allocx == alloc, "where has the allocation gone?");
4931     assert(dest->is_CheckCastPP(), "not an allocation result?");
4932 
4933     _gvn.hash_delete(dest);
4934     dest->set_req(0, control());
4935     Node* destx = _gvn.transform(dest);
4936     assert(destx == dest, "where has the allocation result gone?");
4937   }
4938 }
4939 
4940 
4941 //------------------------------inline_arraycopy-----------------------
4942 // public static native void java.lang.System.arraycopy(Object src,  int  srcPos,
4943 //                                                      Object dest, int destPos,
4944 //                                                      int length);
4945 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_arraycopy() {
4946   // Get the arguments.
4947   Node* src         = argument(0);  // type: oop
4948   Node* src_offset  = argument(1);  // type: int
4949   Node* dest        = argument(2);  // type: oop
4950   Node* dest_offset = argument(3);  // type: int
4951   Node* length      = argument(4);  // type: int
4952 
4953   uint new_idx = C->unique();
4954 
4955   // Check for allocation before we add nodes that would confuse
4956   // tightly_coupled_allocation()
4957   AllocateArrayNode* alloc = tightly_coupled_allocation(dest, NULL);
4958 
4959   int saved_reexecute_sp = -1;
4960   JVMState* saved_jvms = arraycopy_restore_alloc_state(alloc, saved_reexecute_sp);
4961   // See arraycopy_restore_alloc_state() comment
4962   // if alloc == NULL we don't have to worry about a tightly coupled allocation so we can emit all needed guards
4963   // if saved_jvms != NULL (then alloc != NULL) then we can handle guards and a tightly coupled allocation
4964   // if saved_jvms == NULL and alloc != NULL, we can't emit any guards
4965   bool can_emit_guards = (alloc == NULL || saved_jvms != NULL);
4966 
4967   // The following tests must be performed
4968   // (1) src and dest are arrays.
4969   // (2) src and dest arrays must have elements of the same BasicType
4970   // (3) src and dest must not be null.
4971   // (4) src_offset must not be negative.
4972   // (5) dest_offset must not be negative.
4973   // (6) length must not be negative.
4974   // (7) src_offset + length must not exceed length of src.
4975   // (8) dest_offset + length must not exceed length of dest.
4976   // (9) each element of an oop array must be assignable
4977 
4978   // (3) src and dest must not be null.
4979   // always do this here because we need the JVM state for uncommon traps
4980   Node* null_ctl = top();
4981   src  = saved_jvms != NULL ? null_check_oop(src, &null_ctl, true, true) : null_check(src,  T_ARRAY);
4982   assert(null_ctl->is_top(), "no null control here");
4983   dest = null_check(dest, T_ARRAY);
4984 
4985   if (!can_emit_guards) {
4986     // if saved_jvms == NULL and alloc != NULL, we don't emit any
4987     // guards but the arraycopy node could still take advantage of a
4988     // tightly allocated allocation. tightly_coupled_allocation() is
4989     // called again to make sure it takes the null check above into
4990     // account: the null check is mandatory and if it caused an
4991     // uncommon trap to be emitted then the allocation can't be
4992     // considered tightly coupled in this context.
4993     alloc = tightly_coupled_allocation(dest, NULL);
4994   }
4995 
4996   bool validated = false;
4997 
4998   const Type* src_type  = _gvn.type(src);
4999   const Type* dest_type = _gvn.type(dest);
5000   const TypeAryPtr* top_src  = src_type->isa_aryptr();
5001   const TypeAryPtr* top_dest = dest_type->isa_aryptr();
5002 
5003   // Do we have the type of src?
5004   bool has_src = (top_src != NULL && top_src->klass() != NULL);
5005   // Do we have the type of dest?
5006   bool has_dest = (top_dest != NULL && top_dest->klass() != NULL);
5007   // Is the type for src from speculation?
5008   bool src_spec = false;
5009   // Is the type for dest from speculation?
5010   bool dest_spec = false;
5011 
5012   if ((!has_src || !has_dest) && can_emit_guards) {
5013     // We don't have sufficient type information, let's see if
5014     // speculative types can help. We need to have types for both src
5015     // and dest so that it pays off.
5016 
5017     // Do we already have or could we have type information for src
5018     bool could_have_src = has_src;
5019     // Do we already have or could we have type information for dest
5020     bool could_have_dest = has_dest;
5021 
5022     ciKlass* src_k = NULL;
5023     if (!has_src) {
5024       src_k = src_type->speculative_type_not_null();
5025       if (src_k != NULL && src_k->is_array_klass()) {
5026         could_have_src = true;
5027       }
5028     }
5029 
5030     ciKlass* dest_k = NULL;
5031     if (!has_dest) {
5032       dest_k = dest_type->speculative_type_not_null();
5033       if (dest_k != NULL && dest_k->is_array_klass()) {
5034         could_have_dest = true;
5035       }
5036     }
5037 
5038     if (could_have_src && could_have_dest) {
5039       // This is going to pay off so emit the required guards
5040       if (!has_src) {
5041         src = maybe_cast_profiled_obj(src, src_k, true);
5042         src_type  = _gvn.type(src);
5043         top_src  = src_type->isa_aryptr();
5044         has_src = (top_src != NULL && top_src->klass() != NULL);
5045         src_spec = true;
5046       }
5047       if (!has_dest) {
5048         dest = maybe_cast_profiled_obj(dest, dest_k, true);
5049         dest_type  = _gvn.type(dest);
5050         top_dest  = dest_type->isa_aryptr();
5051         has_dest = (top_dest != NULL && top_dest->klass() != NULL);
5052         dest_spec = true;
5053       }
5054     }
5055   }
5056 
5057   if (has_src && has_dest && can_emit_guards) {
5058     BasicType src_elem  = top_src->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5059     BasicType dest_elem = top_dest->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5060     if (src_elem  == T_ARRAY)  src_elem  = T_OBJECT;
5061     if (dest_elem == T_ARRAY)  dest_elem = T_OBJECT;
5062 
5063     if (src_elem == dest_elem && src_elem == T_OBJECT) {
5064       // If both arrays are object arrays then having the exact types
5065       // for both will remove the need for a subtype check at runtime
5066       // before the call and may make it possible to pick a faster copy
5067       // routine (without a subtype check on every element)
5068       // Do we have the exact type of src?
5069       bool could_have_src = src_spec;
5070       // Do we have the exact type of dest?
5071       bool could_have_dest = dest_spec;
5072       ciKlass* src_k = top_src->klass();
5073       ciKlass* dest_k = top_dest->klass();
5074       if (!src_spec) {
5075         src_k = src_type->speculative_type_not_null();
5076         if (src_k != NULL && src_k->is_array_klass()) {
5077           could_have_src = true;
5078         }
5079       }
5080       if (!dest_spec) {
5081         dest_k = dest_type->speculative_type_not_null();
5082         if (dest_k != NULL && dest_k->is_array_klass()) {
5083           could_have_dest = true;
5084         }
5085       }
5086       if (could_have_src && could_have_dest) {
5087         // If we can have both exact types, emit the missing guards
5088         if (could_have_src && !src_spec) {
5089           src = maybe_cast_profiled_obj(src, src_k, true);
5090         }
5091         if (could_have_dest && !dest_spec) {
5092           dest = maybe_cast_profiled_obj(dest, dest_k, true);
5093         }
5094       }
5095     }
5096   }
5097 
5098   ciMethod* trap_method = method();
5099   int trap_bci = bci();
5100   if (saved_jvms != NULL) {
5101     trap_method = alloc->jvms()->method();
5102     trap_bci = alloc->jvms()->bci();
5103   }
5104 
5105   bool negative_length_guard_generated = false;
5106 
5107   if (!C->too_many_traps(trap_method, trap_bci, Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic) &&
5108       can_emit_guards &&
5109       !src->is_top() && !dest->is_top()) {
5110     // validate arguments: enables transformation the ArrayCopyNode
5111     validated = true;
5112 
5113     RegionNode* slow_region = new RegionNode(1);
5114     record_for_igvn(slow_region);
5115 
5116     // (1) src and dest are arrays.
5117     generate_non_array_guard(load_object_klass(src), slow_region);
5118     generate_non_array_guard(load_object_klass(dest), slow_region);
5119 
5120     // (2) src and dest arrays must have elements of the same BasicType
5121     // done at macro expansion or at Ideal transformation time
5122 
5123     // (4) src_offset must not be negative.
5124     generate_negative_guard(src_offset, slow_region);
5125 
5126     // (5) dest_offset must not be negative.
5127     generate_negative_guard(dest_offset, slow_region);
5128 
5129     // (7) src_offset + length must not exceed length of src.
5130     generate_limit_guard(src_offset, length,
5131                          load_array_length(src),
5132                          slow_region);
5133 
5134     // (8) dest_offset + length must not exceed length of dest.
5135     generate_limit_guard(dest_offset, length,
5136                          load_array_length(dest),
5137                          slow_region);
5138 
5139     // (6) length must not be negative.
5140     // This is also checked in generate_arraycopy() during macro expansion, but
5141     // we also have to check it here for the case where the ArrayCopyNode will
5142     // be eliminated by Escape Analysis.
5143     if (EliminateAllocations) {
5144       generate_negative_guard(length, slow_region);
5145       negative_length_guard_generated = true;
5146     }
5147 
5148     // (9) each element of an oop array must be assignable
5149     Node* dest_klass = load_object_klass(dest);
5150     if (src != dest) {
5151       Node* not_subtype_ctrl = gen_subtype_check(src, dest_klass);
5152 
5153       if (not_subtype_ctrl != top()) {
5154         PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
5155         set_control(not_subtype_ctrl);
5156         uncommon_trap(Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic,
5157                       Deoptimization::Action_make_not_entrant);
5158         assert(stopped(), "Should be stopped");
5159       }
5160     }
5161 
5162     const TypeKlassPtr* dest_klass_t = _gvn.type(dest_klass)->is_klassptr();
5163     const Type* toop = TypeOopPtr::make_from_klass(dest_klass_t->klass());
5164     src = _gvn.transform(new CheckCastPPNode(control(), src, toop));
5165     src_type = _gvn.type(src);
5166     top_src  = src_type->isa_aryptr();
5167 
5168     if (top_dest != NULL && !top_dest->elem()->isa_valuetype() && !top_dest->is_not_flat()) {
5169       generate_valueArray_guard(dest_klass, slow_region);
5170     }
5171 
5172     if (top_src != NULL && !top_src->elem()->isa_valuetype() && !top_src->is_not_flat()) {
5173       Node* src_klass = load_object_klass(src);
5174       generate_valueArray_guard(src_klass, slow_region);
5175     }
5176 
5177     {
5178       PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
5179       set_control(_gvn.transform(slow_region));
5180       uncommon_trap(Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic,
5181                     Deoptimization::Action_make_not_entrant);
5182       assert(stopped(), "Should be stopped");
5183     }
5184   }
5185 
5186   arraycopy_move_allocation_here(alloc, dest, saved_jvms, saved_reexecute_sp, new_idx);
5187 
5188   if (stopped()) {
5189     return true;
5190   }
5191 
5192   ArrayCopyNode* ac = ArrayCopyNode::make(this, true, src, src_offset, dest, dest_offset, length, alloc != NULL, negative_length_guard_generated,
5193                                           // Create LoadRange and LoadKlass nodes for use during macro expansion here
5194                                           // so the compiler has a chance to eliminate them: during macro expansion,
5195                                           // we have to set their control (CastPP nodes are eliminated).
5196                                           load_object_klass(src), load_object_klass(dest),
5197                                           load_array_length(src), load_array_length(dest));
5198 
5199   ac->set_arraycopy(validated);
5200 
5201   Node* n = _gvn.transform(ac);
5202   if (n == ac) {
5203     ac->connect_outputs(this);
5204   } else {
5205     assert(validated, "shouldn't transform if all arguments not validated");
5206     set_all_memory(n);
5207   }
5208   clear_upper_avx();
5209 
5210 
5211   return true;
5212 }
5213 
5214 
5215 // Helper function which determines if an arraycopy immediately follows
5216 // an allocation, with no intervening tests or other escapes for the object.
5217 AllocateArrayNode*
5218 LibraryCallKit::tightly_coupled_allocation(Node* ptr,
5219                                            RegionNode* slow_region) {
5220   if (stopped())             return NULL;  // no fast path
5221   if (C->AliasLevel() == 0)  return NULL;  // no MergeMems around
5222 
5223   AllocateArrayNode* alloc = AllocateArrayNode::Ideal_array_allocation(ptr, &_gvn);
5224   if (alloc == NULL)  return NULL;
5225 
5226   Node* rawmem = memory(Compile::AliasIdxRaw);
5227   // Is the allocation's memory state untouched?
5228   if (!(rawmem->is_Proj() && rawmem->in(0)->is_Initialize())) {
5229     // Bail out if there have been raw-memory effects since the allocation.
5230     // (Example:  There might have been a call or safepoint.)
5231     return NULL;
5232   }
5233   rawmem = rawmem->in(0)->as_Initialize()->memory(Compile::AliasIdxRaw);
5234   if (!(rawmem->is_Proj() && rawmem->in(0) == alloc)) {
5235     return NULL;
5236   }
5237 
5238   // There must be no unexpected observers of this allocation.
5239   for (DUIterator_Fast imax, i = ptr->fast_outs(imax); i < imax; i++) {
5240     Node* obs = ptr->fast_out(i);
5241     if (obs != this->map()) {
5242       return NULL;
5243     }
5244   }
5245 
5246   // This arraycopy must unconditionally follow the allocation of the ptr.
5247   Node* alloc_ctl = ptr->in(0);
5248   Node* ctl = control();
5249   while (ctl != alloc_ctl) {
5250     // There may be guards which feed into the slow_region.
5251     // Any other control flow means that we might not get a chance
5252     // to finish initializing the allocated object.
5253     if ((ctl->is_IfFalse() || ctl->is_IfTrue()) && ctl->in(0)->is_If()) {
5254       IfNode* iff = ctl->in(0)->as_If();
5255       Node* not_ctl = iff->proj_out_or_null(1 - ctl->as_Proj()->_con);
5256       assert(not_ctl != NULL && not_ctl != ctl, "found alternate");
5257       if (slow_region != NULL && slow_region->find_edge(not_ctl) >= 1) {
5258         ctl = iff->in(0);       // This test feeds the known slow_region.
5259         continue;
5260       }
5261       // One more try:  Various low-level checks bottom out in
5262       // uncommon traps.  If the debug-info of the trap omits
5263       // any reference to the allocation, as we've already
5264       // observed, then there can be no objection to the trap.
5265       bool found_trap = false;
5266       for (DUIterator_Fast jmax, j = not_ctl->fast_outs(jmax); j < jmax; j++) {
5267         Node* obs = not_ctl->fast_out(j);
5268         if (obs->in(0) == not_ctl && obs->is_Call() &&
5269             (obs->as_Call()->entry_point() == SharedRuntime::uncommon_trap_blob()->entry_point())) {
5270           found_trap = true; break;
5271         }
5272       }
5273       if (found_trap) {
5274         ctl = iff->in(0);       // This test feeds a harmless uncommon trap.
5275         continue;
5276       }
5277     }
5278     return NULL;
5279   }
5280 
5281   // If we get this far, we have an allocation which immediately
5282   // precedes the arraycopy, and we can take over zeroing the new object.
5283   // The arraycopy will finish the initialization, and provide
5284   // a new control state to which we will anchor the destination pointer.
5285 
5286   return alloc;
5287 }
5288 
5289 //-------------inline_encodeISOArray-----------------------------------
5290 // encode char[] to byte[] in ISO_8859_1
5291 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_encodeISOArray() {
5292   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 5, "encodeISOArray has 5 parameters");
5293   // no receiver since it is static method
5294   Node *src         = argument(0);
5295   Node *src_offset  = argument(1);
5296   Node *dst         = argument(2);
5297   Node *dst_offset  = argument(3);
5298   Node *length      = argument(4);
5299 
5300   src = must_be_not_null(src, true);
5301   dst = must_be_not_null(dst, true);
5302 
5303   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
5304   const Type* dst_type = dst->Value(&_gvn);
5305   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
5306   const TypeAryPtr* top_dest = dst_type->isa_aryptr();
5307   if (top_src  == NULL || top_src->klass()  == NULL ||
5308       top_dest == NULL || top_dest->klass() == NULL) {
5309     // failed array check
5310     return false;
5311   }
5312 
5313   // Figure out the size and type of the elements we will be copying.
5314   BasicType src_elem = src_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5315   BasicType dst_elem = dst_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5316   if (!((src_elem == T_CHAR) || (src_elem== T_BYTE)) || dst_elem != T_BYTE) {
5317     return false;
5318   }
5319 
5320   Node* src_start = array_element_address(src, src_offset, T_CHAR);
5321   Node* dst_start = array_element_address(dst, dst_offset, dst_elem);
5322   // 'src_start' points to src array + scaled offset
5323   // 'dst_start' points to dst array + scaled offset
5324 
5325   const TypeAryPtr* mtype = TypeAryPtr::BYTES;
5326   Node* enc = new EncodeISOArrayNode(control(), memory(mtype), src_start, dst_start, length);
5327   enc = _gvn.transform(enc);
5328   Node* res_mem = _gvn.transform(new SCMemProjNode(enc));
5329   set_memory(res_mem, mtype);
5330   set_result(enc);
5331   clear_upper_avx();
5332 
5333   return true;
5334 }
5335 
5336 //-------------inline_multiplyToLen-----------------------------------
5337 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_multiplyToLen() {
5338   assert(UseMultiplyToLenIntrinsic, "not implemented on this platform");
5339 
5340   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::multiplyToLen();
5341   if (stubAddr == NULL) {
5342     return false; // Intrinsic's stub is not implemented on this platform
5343   }
5344   const char* stubName = "multiplyToLen";
5345 
5346   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 5, "multiplyToLen has 5 parameters");
5347 
5348   // no receiver because it is a static method
5349   Node* x    = argument(0);
5350   Node* xlen = argument(1);
5351   Node* y    = argument(2);
5352   Node* ylen = argument(3);
5353   Node* z    = argument(4);
5354 
5355   x = must_be_not_null(x, true);
5356   y = must_be_not_null(y, true);
5357 
5358   const Type* x_type = x->Value(&_gvn);
5359   const Type* y_type = y->Value(&_gvn);
5360   const TypeAryPtr* top_x = x_type->isa_aryptr();
5361   const TypeAryPtr* top_y = y_type->isa_aryptr();
5362   if (top_x  == NULL || top_x->klass()  == NULL ||
5363       top_y == NULL || top_y->klass() == NULL) {
5364     // failed array check
5365     return false;
5366   }
5367 
5368   BasicType x_elem = x_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5369   BasicType y_elem = y_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5370   if (x_elem != T_INT || y_elem != T_INT) {
5371     return false;
5372   }
5373 
5374   // Set the original stack and the reexecute bit for the interpreter to reexecute
5375   // the bytecode that invokes BigInteger.multiplyToLen() if deoptimization happens
5376   // on the return from z array allocation in runtime.
5377   { PreserveReexecuteState preexecs(this);
5378     jvms()->set_should_reexecute(true);
5379 
5380     Node* x_start = array_element_address(x, intcon(0), x_elem);
5381     Node* y_start = array_element_address(y, intcon(0), y_elem);
5382     // 'x_start' points to x array + scaled xlen
5383     // 'y_start' points to y array + scaled ylen
5384 
5385     // Allocate the result array
5386     Node* zlen = _gvn.transform(new AddINode(xlen, ylen));
5387     ciKlass* klass = ciTypeArrayKlass::make(T_INT);
5388     Node* klass_node = makecon(TypeKlassPtr::make(klass));
5389 
5390     IdealKit ideal(this);
5391 
5392 #define __ ideal.
5393      Node* one = __ ConI(1);
5394      Node* zero = __ ConI(0);
5395      IdealVariable need_alloc(ideal), z_alloc(ideal);  __ declarations_done();
5396      __ set(need_alloc, zero);
5397      __ set(z_alloc, z);
5398      __ if_then(z, BoolTest::eq, null()); {
5399        __ increment (need_alloc, one);
5400      } __ else_(); {
5401        // Update graphKit memory and control from IdealKit.
5402        sync_kit(ideal);
5403        Node *cast = new CastPPNode(z, TypePtr::NOTNULL);
5404        cast->init_req(0, control());
5405        _gvn.set_type(cast, cast->bottom_type());
5406        C->record_for_igvn(cast);
5407 
5408        Node* zlen_arg = load_array_length(cast);
5409        // Update IdealKit memory and control from graphKit.
5410        __ sync_kit(this);
5411        __ if_then(zlen_arg, BoolTest::lt, zlen); {
5412          __ increment (need_alloc, one);
5413        } __ end_if();
5414      } __ end_if();
5415 
5416      __ if_then(__ value(need_alloc), BoolTest::ne, zero); {
5417        // Update graphKit memory and control from IdealKit.
5418        sync_kit(ideal);
5419        Node * narr = new_array(klass_node, zlen, 1);
5420        // Update IdealKit memory and control from graphKit.
5421        __ sync_kit(this);
5422        __ set(z_alloc, narr);
5423      } __ end_if();
5424 
5425      sync_kit(ideal);
5426      z = __ value(z_alloc);
5427      // Can't use TypeAryPtr::INTS which uses Bottom offset.
5428      _gvn.set_type(z, TypeOopPtr::make_from_klass(klass));
5429      // Final sync IdealKit and GraphKit.
5430      final_sync(ideal);
5431 #undef __
5432 
5433     Node* z_start = array_element_address(z, intcon(0), T_INT);
5434 
5435     Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
5436                                    OptoRuntime::multiplyToLen_Type(),
5437                                    stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5438                                    x_start, xlen, y_start, ylen, z_start, zlen);
5439   } // original reexecute is set back here
5440 
5441   C->set_has_split_ifs(true); // Has chance for split-if optimization
5442   set_result(z);
5443   return true;
5444 }

5485

5548   if (stubAddr == NULL) {

5561   Node* inv  = argument(4);
5562   Node* m    = argument(6);
5563 
5564   const Type* a_type = a->Value(&_gvn);
5565   const TypeAryPtr* top_a = a_type->isa_aryptr();
5566   const Type* b_type = b->Value(&_gvn);

5568   const Type* n_type = a->Value(&_gvn);

5570   const Type* m_type = a->Value(&_gvn);
5571   const TypeAryPtr* top_m = m_type->isa_aryptr();
5572   if (top_a  == NULL || top_a->klass()  == NULL ||
5573       top_b == NULL || top_b->klass()  == NULL ||
5574       top_n == NULL || top_n->klass()  == NULL ||
5575       top_m == NULL || top_m->klass()  == NULL) {
5576     // failed array check
5577     return false;
5578   }
5579

5581   BasicType b_elem = b_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5582   BasicType n_elem = n_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5583   BasicType m_elem = m_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();

5589   {
5590     Node* a_start = array_element_address(a, intcon(0), a_elem);
5591     Node* b_start = array_element_address(b, intcon(0), b_elem);
5592     Node* n_start = array_element_address(n, intcon(0), n_elem);
5593     Node* m_start = array_element_address(m, intcon(0), m_elem);
5594

5596                                    OptoRuntime::montgomeryMultiply_Type(),
5597                                    stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5598                                    a_start, b_start, n_start, len, inv, top(),
5599                                    m_start);

5660 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_bigIntegerShift(bool isRightShift) {
5661   address stubAddr = NULL;
5662   const char* stubName = NULL;
5663 
5664   stubAddr = isRightShift? StubRoutines::bigIntegerRightShift(): StubRoutines::bigIntegerLeftShift();
5665   if (stubAddr == NULL) {
5666     return false; // Intrinsic's stub is not implemented on this platform
5667   }
5668 
5669   stubName = isRightShift? "bigIntegerRightShiftWorker" : "bigIntegerLeftShiftWorker";
5670 
5671   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 5, "expected 5 arguments");
5672 
5673   Node* newArr = argument(0);
5674   Node* oldArr = argument(1);
5675   Node* newIdx = argument(2);
5676   Node* shiftCount = argument(3);
5677   Node* numIter = argument(4);
5678 
5679   const Type* newArr_type = newArr->Value(&_gvn);
5680   const TypeAryPtr* top_newArr = newArr_type->isa_aryptr();
5681   const Type* oldArr_type = oldArr->Value(&_gvn);
5682   const TypeAryPtr* top_oldArr = oldArr_type->isa_aryptr();
5683   if (top_newArr == NULL || top_newArr->klass() == NULL || top_oldArr == NULL
5684       || top_oldArr->klass() == NULL) {
5685     return false;
5686   }
5687 
5688   BasicType newArr_elem = newArr_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5689   BasicType oldArr_elem = oldArr_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5690   if (newArr_elem != T_INT || oldArr_elem != T_INT) {
5691     return false;
5692   }
5693 
5694   // Make the call
5695   {
5696     Node* newArr_start = array_element_address(newArr, intcon(0), newArr_elem);
5697     Node* oldArr_start = array_element_address(oldArr, intcon(0), oldArr_elem);
5698 
5699     Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF,
5700                                    OptoRuntime::bigIntegerShift_Type(),
5701                                    stubAddr,
5702                                    stubName,
5703                                    TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5704                                    newArr_start,
5705                                    oldArr_start,
5706                                    newIdx,
5707                                    shiftCount,
5708                                    numIter);
5709   }
5710 
5711   return true;
5712 }

5759 /**
5760  * Calculate CRC32 for byte.
5761  * int java.util.zip.CRC32.update(int crc, int b)
5762  */
5763 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_updateCRC32() {
5764   assert(UseCRC32Intrinsics, "need AVX and LCMUL instructions support");
5765   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 2, "update has 2 parameters");
5766   // no receiver since it is static method
5767   Node* crc  = argument(0); // type: int
5768   Node* b    = argument(1); // type: int
5769 
5770   /*
5771    *    int c = ~ crc;
5772    *    b = timesXtoThe32[(b ^ c) & 0xFF];
5773    *    b = b ^ (c >>> 8);
5774    *    crc = ~b;
5775    */
5776 
5777   Node* M1 = intcon(-1);
5778   crc = _gvn.transform(new XorINode(crc, M1));
5779   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new XorINode(crc, b));
5780   result = _gvn.transform(new AndINode(result, intcon(0xFF)));
5781 
5782   Node* base = makecon(TypeRawPtr::make(StubRoutines::crc_table_addr()));
5783   Node* offset = _gvn.transform(new LShiftINode(result, intcon(0x2)));
5784   Node* adr = basic_plus_adr(top(), base, ConvI2X(offset));
5785   result = make_load(control(), adr, TypeInt::INT, T_INT, MemNode::unordered);
5786 
5787   crc = _gvn.transform(new URShiftINode(crc, intcon(8)));
5788   result = _gvn.transform(new XorINode(crc, result));
5789   result = _gvn.transform(new XorINode(result, M1));
5790   set_result(result);
5791   return true;
5792 }
5793 
5794 /**
5795  * Calculate CRC32 for byte[] array.
5796  * int java.util.zip.CRC32.updateBytes(int crc, byte[] buf, int off, int len)
5797  */
5798 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_updateBytesCRC32() {
5799   assert(UseCRC32Intrinsics, "need AVX and LCMUL instructions support");
5800   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 4, "updateBytes has 4 parameters");
5801   // no receiver since it is static method
5802   Node* crc     = argument(0); // type: int
5803   Node* src     = argument(1); // type: oop
5804   Node* offset  = argument(2); // type: int
5805   Node* length  = argument(3); // type: int
5806 
5807   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
5808   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
5809   if (top_src  == NULL || top_src->klass()  == NULL) {
5810     // failed array check
5811     return false;
5812   }
5813 
5814   // Figure out the size and type of the elements we will be copying.
5815   BasicType src_elem = src_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5816   if (src_elem != T_BYTE) {
5817     return false;
5818   }
5819 
5820   // 'src_start' points to src array + scaled offset
5821   src = must_be_not_null(src, true);
5822   Node* src_start = array_element_address(src, offset, src_elem);
5823 
5824   // We assume that range check is done by caller.
5825   // TODO: generate range check (offset+length < src.length) in debug VM.
5826 
5827   // Call the stub.
5828   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::updateBytesCRC32();
5829   const char *stubName = "updateBytesCRC32";
5830 
5831   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP, OptoRuntime::updateBytesCRC32_Type(),
5832                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5833                                  crc, src_start, length);
5834   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(call, TypeFunc::Parms));
5835   set_result(result);
5836   return true;
5837 }

5839 /**
5840  * Calculate CRC32 for ByteBuffer.
5841  * int java.util.zip.CRC32.updateByteBuffer(int crc, long buf, int off, int len)
5842  */
5843 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_updateByteBufferCRC32() {
5844   assert(UseCRC32Intrinsics, "need AVX and LCMUL instructions support");
5845   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 5, "updateByteBuffer has 4 parameters and one is long");
5846   // no receiver since it is static method
5847   Node* crc     = argument(0); // type: int
5848   Node* src     = argument(1); // type: long
5849   Node* offset  = argument(3); // type: int
5850   Node* length  = argument(4); // type: int
5851 
5852   src = ConvL2X(src);  // adjust Java long to machine word
5853   Node* base = _gvn.transform(new CastX2PNode(src));
5854   offset = ConvI2X(offset);
5855 
5856   // 'src_start' points to src array + scaled offset
5857   Node* src_start = basic_plus_adr(top(), base, offset);
5858 
5859   // Call the stub.
5860   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::updateBytesCRC32();
5861   const char *stubName = "updateBytesCRC32";
5862 
5863   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP, OptoRuntime::updateBytesCRC32_Type(),
5864                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5865                                  crc, src_start, length);
5866   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(call, TypeFunc::Parms));
5867   set_result(result);
5868   return true;
5869 }

5871 //------------------------------get_table_from_crc32c_class-----------------------
5872 Node * LibraryCallKit::get_table_from_crc32c_class(ciInstanceKlass *crc32c_class) {
5873   Node* table = load_field_from_object(NULL, "byteTable", "[I", /*is_exact*/ false, /*is_static*/ true, crc32c_class);
5874   assert (table != NULL, "wrong version of java.util.zip.CRC32C");
5875 
5876   return table;
5877 }
