5879 //------------------------------inline_updateBytesCRC32C-----------------------
5880 //
5881 // Calculate CRC32C for byte[] array.
5882 // int java.util.zip.CRC32C.updateBytes(int crc, byte[] buf, int off, int end)
5883 //
5884 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_updateBytesCRC32C() {
5885   assert(UseCRC32CIntrinsics, "need CRC32C instruction support");
5886   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 4, "updateBytes has 4 parameters");
5887   assert(callee()->holder()->is_loaded(), "CRC32C class must be loaded");
5888   // no receiver since it is a static method
5889   Node* crc     = argument(0); // type: int
5890   Node* src     = argument(1); // type: oop
5891   Node* offset  = argument(2); // type: int
5892   Node* end     = argument(3); // type: int
5893 
5894   Node* length = _gvn.transform(new SubINode(end, offset));
5895 
5896   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
5897   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
5898   if (top_src  == NULL || top_src->klass()  == NULL) {
5899     // failed array check
5900     return false;
5901   }
5902 
5903   // Figure out the size and type of the elements we will be copying.
5904   BasicType src_elem = src_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5905   if (src_elem != T_BYTE) {
5906     return false;
5907   }
5908 
5909   // 'src_start' points to src array + scaled offset
5910   src = must_be_not_null(src, true);
5911   Node* src_start = array_element_address(src, offset, src_elem);
5912 
5913   // static final int[] byteTable in class CRC32C
5914   Node* table = get_table_from_crc32c_class(callee()->holder());
5915   table = must_be_not_null(table, true);
5916   Node* table_start = array_element_address(table, intcon(0), T_INT);
5917 
5918   // We assume that range check is done by caller.
5919   // TODO: generate range check (offset+length < src.length) in debug VM.
5920 
5921   // Call the stub.
5922   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::updateBytesCRC32C();
5923   const char *stubName = "updateBytesCRC32C";
5924 
5925   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF, OptoRuntime::updateBytesCRC32C_Type(),
5926                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5927                                  crc, src_start, length, table_start);
5928   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(call, TypeFunc::Parms));
5929   set_result(result);
5930   return true;
5931 }

5933 //------------------------------inline_updateDirectByteBufferCRC32C-----------------------
5934 //
5935 // Calculate CRC32C for DirectByteBuffer.
5936 // int java.util.zip.CRC32C.updateDirectByteBuffer(int crc, long buf, int off, int end)
5937 //
5938 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_updateDirectByteBufferCRC32C() {
5939   assert(UseCRC32CIntrinsics, "need CRC32C instruction support");
5940   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 5, "updateDirectByteBuffer has 4 parameters and one is long");
5941   assert(callee()->holder()->is_loaded(), "CRC32C class must be loaded");
5942   // no receiver since it is a static method
5943   Node* crc     = argument(0); // type: int
5944   Node* src     = argument(1); // type: long
5945   Node* offset  = argument(3); // type: int
5946   Node* end     = argument(4); // type: int
5947 
5948   Node* length = _gvn.transform(new SubINode(end, offset));
5949 
5950   src = ConvL2X(src);  // adjust Java long to machine word
5951   Node* base = _gvn.transform(new CastX2PNode(src));
5952   offset = ConvI2X(offset);
5953 
5954   // 'src_start' points to src array + scaled offset
5955   Node* src_start = basic_plus_adr(top(), base, offset);
5956 
5957   // static final int[] byteTable in class CRC32C
5958   Node* table = get_table_from_crc32c_class(callee()->holder());
5959   table = must_be_not_null(table, true);
5960   Node* table_start = array_element_address(table, intcon(0), T_INT);
5961 
5962   // Call the stub.
5963   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::updateBytesCRC32C();
5964   const char *stubName = "updateBytesCRC32C";
5965 
5966   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF, OptoRuntime::updateBytesCRC32C_Type(),
5967                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5968                                  crc, src_start, length, table_start);
5969   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(call, TypeFunc::Parms));
5970   set_result(result);
5971   return true;
5972 }
5973 
5974 //------------------------------inline_updateBytesAdler32----------------------
5975 //
5976 // Calculate Adler32 checksum for byte[] array.
5977 // int java.util.zip.Adler32.updateBytes(int crc, byte[] buf, int off, int len)
5978 //
5979 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_updateBytesAdler32() {
5980   assert(UseAdler32Intrinsics, "Adler32 Instrinsic support need"); // check if we actually need to check this flag or check a different one
5981   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 4, "updateBytes has 4 parameters");
5982   assert(callee()->holder()->is_loaded(), "Adler32 class must be loaded");
5983   // no receiver since it is static method
5984   Node* crc     = argument(0); // type: int
5985   Node* src     = argument(1); // type: oop
5986   Node* offset  = argument(2); // type: int
5987   Node* length  = argument(3); // type: int
5988 
5989   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
5990   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
5991   if (top_src  == NULL || top_src->klass()  == NULL) {
5992     // failed array check
5993     return false;
5994   }
5995 
5996   // Figure out the size and type of the elements we will be copying.
5997   BasicType src_elem = src_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5998   if (src_elem != T_BYTE) {
5999     return false;
6000   }
6001 
6002   // 'src_start' points to src array + scaled offset
6003   Node* src_start = array_element_address(src, offset, src_elem);
6004 
6005   // We assume that range check is done by caller.
6006   // TODO: generate range check (offset+length < src.length) in debug VM.
6007 
6008   // Call the stub.
6009   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::updateBytesAdler32();
6010   const char *stubName = "updateBytesAdler32";
6011 
6012   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF, OptoRuntime::updateBytesAdler32_Type(),
6013                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6014                                  crc, src_start, length);
6015   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(call, TypeFunc::Parms));
6016   set_result(result);
6017   return true;
6018 }
6019 
6020 //------------------------------inline_updateByteBufferAdler32---------------
6021 //
6022 // Calculate Adler32 checksum for DirectByteBuffer.
6023 // int java.util.zip.Adler32.updateByteBuffer(int crc, long buf, int off, int len)
6024 //
6025 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_updateByteBufferAdler32() {
6026   assert(UseAdler32Intrinsics, "Adler32 Instrinsic support need"); // check if we actually need to check this flag or check a different one
6027   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 5, "updateByteBuffer has 4 parameters and one is long");
6028   assert(callee()->holder()->is_loaded(), "Adler32 class must be loaded");
6029   // no receiver since it is static method
6030   Node* crc     = argument(0); // type: int
6031   Node* src     = argument(1); // type: long
6032   Node* offset  = argument(3); // type: int
6033   Node* length  = argument(4); // type: int
6034 
6035   src = ConvL2X(src);  // adjust Java long to machine word
6036   Node* base = _gvn.transform(new CastX2PNode(src));
6037   offset = ConvI2X(offset);
6038 
6039   // 'src_start' points to src array + scaled offset
6040   Node* src_start = basic_plus_adr(top(), base, offset);
6041 
6042   // Call the stub.
6043   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::updateBytesAdler32();
6044   const char *stubName = "updateBytesAdler32";
6045 
6046   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF, OptoRuntime::updateBytesAdler32_Type(),
6047                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6048                                  crc, src_start, length);
6049 
6050   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(call, TypeFunc::Parms));
6051   set_result(result);
6052   return true;
6053 }
6054 
6055 //----------------------------inline_reference_get----------------------------
6056 // public T java.lang.ref.Reference.get();
6057 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_reference_get() {
6058   const int referent_offset = java_lang_ref_Reference::referent_offset;
6059   guarantee(referent_offset > 0, "should have already been set");
6060 
6061   // Get the argument:
6062   Node* reference_obj = null_check_receiver();
6063   if (stopped()) return true;
6064 
6065   const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(reference_obj)->isa_instptr();
6066   assert(tinst != NULL, "obj is null");
6067   assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "obj is not loaded");
6068   ciInstanceKlass* referenceKlass = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass();
6069   ciField* field = referenceKlass->get_field_by_name(ciSymbol::make("referent"),
6070                                                      ciSymbol::make("Ljava/lang/Object;"),
6071                                                      false);
6072   assert (field != NULL, "undefined field");
6073 
6074   Node* adr = basic_plus_adr(reference_obj, reference_obj, referent_offset);
6075   const TypePtr* adr_type = C->alias_type(field)->adr_type();
6076 
6077   ciInstanceKlass* klass = env()->Object_klass();
6078   const TypeOopPtr* object_type = TypeOopPtr::make_from_klass(klass);
6079 
6080   DecoratorSet decorators = IN_HEAP | ON_WEAK_OOP_REF;
6081   Node* result = access_load_at(reference_obj, adr, adr_type, object_type, T_OBJECT, decorators);
6082   // Add memory barrier to prevent commoning reads from this field
6083   // across safepoint since GC can change its value.
6084   insert_mem_bar(Op_MemBarCPUOrder);
6085 
6086   set_result(result);
6087   return true;
6088 }
6089 
6090 
6091 Node * LibraryCallKit::load_field_from_object(Node * fromObj, const char * fieldName, const char * fieldTypeString,
6092                                               bool is_exact=true, bool is_static=false,
6093                                               ciInstanceKlass * fromKls=NULL) {
6094   if (fromKls == NULL) {
6095     const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(fromObj)->isa_instptr();
6096     assert(tinst != NULL, "obj is null");
6097     assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "obj is not loaded");
6098     assert(!is_exact || tinst->klass_is_exact(), "klass not exact");
6099     fromKls = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass();
6100   } else {
6101     assert(is_static, "only for static field access");
6102   }
6103   ciField* field = fromKls->get_field_by_name(ciSymbol::make(fieldName),
6104                                               ciSymbol::make(fieldTypeString),
6105                                               is_static);
6106 
6107   assert (field != NULL, "undefined field");
6108   if (field == NULL) return (Node *) NULL;
6109 
6110   if (is_static) {
6111     const TypeInstPtr* tip = TypeInstPtr::make(fromKls->java_mirror());
6112     fromObj = makecon(tip);
6113   }
6114 
6115   // Next code  copied from Parse::do_get_xxx():
6116 
6117   // Compute address and memory type.
6118   int offset  = field->offset_in_bytes();
6119   bool is_vol = field->is_volatile();
6120   ciType* field_klass = field->type();
6121   assert(field_klass->is_loaded(), "should be loaded");
6122   const TypePtr* adr_type = C->alias_type(field)->adr_type();
6123   Node *adr = basic_plus_adr(fromObj, fromObj, offset);
6124   BasicType bt = field->layout_type();
6125 
6126   // Build the resultant type of the load
6127   const Type *type;
6128   if (bt == T_OBJECT) {
6129     type = TypeOopPtr::make_from_klass(field_klass->as_klass());
6130   } else {
6131     type = Type::get_const_basic_type(bt);
6132   }
6133 
6134   DecoratorSet decorators = IN_HEAP;
6135 
6136   if (is_vol) {
6137     decorators |= MO_SEQ_CST;
6138   }
6139 
6140   return access_load_at(fromObj, adr, adr_type, type, bt, decorators);
6141 }
6142 
6143 Node * LibraryCallKit::field_address_from_object(Node * fromObj, const char * fieldName, const char * fieldTypeString,
6144                                                  bool is_exact = true, bool is_static = false,
6145                                                  ciInstanceKlass * fromKls = NULL) {
6146   if (fromKls == NULL) {
6147     const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(fromObj)->isa_instptr();
6148     assert(tinst != NULL, "obj is null");
6149     assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "obj is not loaded");
6150     assert(!is_exact || tinst->klass_is_exact(), "klass not exact");
6151     fromKls = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass();
6152   }
6153   else {
6154     assert(is_static, "only for static field access");
6155   }
6156   ciField* field = fromKls->get_field_by_name(ciSymbol::make(fieldName),
6157     ciSymbol::make(fieldTypeString),
6158     is_static);
6159 
6160   assert(field != NULL, "undefined field");
6161   assert(!field->is_volatile(), "not defined for volatile fields");
6162 
6163   if (is_static) {
6164     const TypeInstPtr* tip = TypeInstPtr::make(fromKls->java_mirror());
6165     fromObj = makecon(tip);
6166   }
6167 
6168   // Next code  copied from Parse::do_get_xxx():
6169 
6170   // Compute address and memory type.
6171   int offset = field->offset_in_bytes();
6172   Node *adr = basic_plus_adr(fromObj, fromObj, offset);
6173 
6174   return adr;
6175 }

6177 //------------------------------inline_aescrypt_Block-----------------------
6178 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_aescrypt_Block(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
6179   address stubAddr = NULL;
6180   const char *stubName;
6181   assert(UseAES, "need AES instruction support");
6182 
6183   switch(id) {
6184   case vmIntrinsics::_aescrypt_encryptBlock:
6185     stubAddr = StubRoutines::aescrypt_encryptBlock();
6186     stubName = "aescrypt_encryptBlock";
6187     break;
6188   case vmIntrinsics::_aescrypt_decryptBlock:
6189     stubAddr = StubRoutines::aescrypt_decryptBlock();
6190     stubName = "aescrypt_decryptBlock";
6191     break;
6192   default:
6193     break;
6194   }
6195   if (stubAddr == NULL) return false;
6196 
6197   Node* aescrypt_object = argument(0);
6198   Node* src             = argument(1);
6199   Node* src_offset      = argument(2);
6200   Node* dest            = argument(3);
6201   Node* dest_offset     = argument(4);
6202 
6203   src = must_be_not_null(src, true);
6204   dest = must_be_not_null(dest, true);
6205 
6206   // (1) src and dest are arrays.
6207   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
6208   const Type* dest_type = dest->Value(&_gvn);
6209   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
6210   const TypeAryPtr* top_dest = dest_type->isa_aryptr();
6211   assert (top_src  != NULL && top_src->klass()  != NULL &&  top_dest != NULL && top_dest->klass() != NULL, "args are strange");
6212 
6213   // for the quick and dirty code we will skip all the checks.
6214   // we are just trying to get the call to be generated.
6215   Node* src_start  = src;
6216   Node* dest_start = dest;
6217   if (src_offset != NULL || dest_offset != NULL) {
6218     assert(src_offset != NULL && dest_offset != NULL, "");
6219     src_start  = array_element_address(src,  src_offset,  T_BYTE);
6220     dest_start = array_element_address(dest, dest_offset, T_BYTE);
6221   }
6222 
6223   // now need to get the start of its expanded key array
6224   // this requires a newer class file that has this array as littleEndian ints, otherwise we revert to java
6225   Node* k_start = get_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(aescrypt_object);
6226   if (k_start == NULL) return false;
6227 
6228   if (Matcher::pass_original_key_for_aes()) {
6229     // on SPARC we need to pass the original key since key expansion needs to happen in intrinsics due to
6230     // compatibility issues between Java key expansion and SPARC crypto instructions
6231     Node* original_k_start = get_original_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(aescrypt_object);
6232     if (original_k_start == NULL) return false;
6233 
6234     // Call the stub.
6235     make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP, OptoRuntime::aescrypt_block_Type(),
6236                       stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6237                       src_start, dest_start, k_start, original_k_start);
6238   } else {
6239     // Call the stub.
6240     make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP, OptoRuntime::aescrypt_block_Type(),
6241                       stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6242                       src_start, dest_start, k_start);
6243   }
6244 
6245   return true;
6246 }
6247 
6248 //------------------------------inline_cipherBlockChaining_AESCrypt-----------------------
6249 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_cipherBlockChaining_AESCrypt(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
6250   address stubAddr = NULL;
6251   const char *stubName = NULL;
6252 
6253   assert(UseAES, "need AES instruction support");
6254 
6255   switch(id) {
6256   case vmIntrinsics::_cipherBlockChaining_encryptAESCrypt:
6257     stubAddr = StubRoutines::cipherBlockChaining_encryptAESCrypt();
6258     stubName = "cipherBlockChaining_encryptAESCrypt";
6259     break;
6260   case vmIntrinsics::_cipherBlockChaining_decryptAESCrypt:
6261     stubAddr = StubRoutines::cipherBlockChaining_decryptAESCrypt();
6262     stubName = "cipherBlockChaining_decryptAESCrypt";
6263     break;
6264   default:
6265     break;
6266   }
6267   if (stubAddr == NULL) return false;
6268 
6269   Node* cipherBlockChaining_object = argument(0);
6270   Node* src                        = argument(1);
6271   Node* src_offset                 = argument(2);
6272   Node* len                        = argument(3);
6273   Node* dest                       = argument(4);
6274   Node* dest_offset                = argument(5);
6275 
6276   src = must_be_not_null(src, false);
6277   dest = must_be_not_null(dest, false);
6278 
6279   // (1) src and dest are arrays.
6280   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
6281   const Type* dest_type = dest->Value(&_gvn);
6282   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
6283   const TypeAryPtr* top_dest = dest_type->isa_aryptr();
6284   assert (top_src  != NULL && top_src->klass()  != NULL
6285           &&  top_dest != NULL && top_dest->klass() != NULL, "args are strange");
6286 
6287   // checks are the responsibility of the caller
6288   Node* src_start  = src;
6289   Node* dest_start = dest;
6290   if (src_offset != NULL || dest_offset != NULL) {
6291     assert(src_offset != NULL && dest_offset != NULL, "");
6292     src_start  = array_element_address(src,  src_offset,  T_BYTE);
6293     dest_start = array_element_address(dest, dest_offset, T_BYTE);
6294   }
6295 
6296   // if we are in this set of code, we "know" the embeddedCipher is an AESCrypt object
6297   // (because of the predicated logic executed earlier).
6298   // so we cast it here safely.
6299   // this requires a newer class file that has this array as littleEndian ints, otherwise we revert to java
6300 
6301   Node* embeddedCipherObj = load_field_from_object(cipherBlockChaining_object, "embeddedCipher", "Lcom/sun/crypto/provider/SymmetricCipher;", /*is_exact*/ false);
6302   if (embeddedCipherObj == NULL) return false;
6303 
6304   // cast it to what we know it will be at runtime
6305   const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(cipherBlockChaining_object)->isa_instptr();
6306   assert(tinst != NULL, "CBC obj is null");
6307   assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "CBC obj is not loaded");
6308   ciKlass* klass_AESCrypt = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass()->find_klass(ciSymbol::make("com/sun/crypto/provider/AESCrypt"));
6309   assert(klass_AESCrypt->is_loaded(), "predicate checks that this class is loaded");
6310 
6311   ciInstanceKlass* instklass_AESCrypt = klass_AESCrypt->as_instance_klass();
6312   const TypeKlassPtr* aklass = TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_AESCrypt);
6313   const TypeOopPtr* xtype = aklass->as_instance_type();
6314   Node* aescrypt_object = new CheckCastPPNode(control(), embeddedCipherObj, xtype);
6315   aescrypt_object = _gvn.transform(aescrypt_object);
6316 
6317   // we need to get the start of the aescrypt_object's expanded key array
6318   Node* k_start = get_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(aescrypt_object);
6319   if (k_start == NULL) return false;
6320 
6321   // similarly, get the start address of the r vector
6322   Node* objRvec = load_field_from_object(cipherBlockChaining_object, "r", "[B", /*is_exact*/ false);
6323   if (objRvec == NULL) return false;
6324   Node* r_start = array_element_address(objRvec, intcon(0), T_BYTE);
6325 
6326   Node* cbcCrypt;
6327   if (Matcher::pass_original_key_for_aes()) {
6328     // on SPARC we need to pass the original key since key expansion needs to happen in intrinsics due to
6329     // compatibility issues between Java key expansion and SPARC crypto instructions
6330     Node* original_k_start = get_original_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(aescrypt_object);
6331     if (original_k_start == NULL) return false;
6332 
6333     // Call the stub, passing src_start, dest_start, k_start, r_start, src_len and original_k_start
6334     cbcCrypt = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
6335                                  OptoRuntime::cipherBlockChaining_aescrypt_Type(),
6336                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6337                                  src_start, dest_start, k_start, r_start, len, original_k_start);
6338   } else {
6339     // Call the stub, passing src_start, dest_start, k_start, r_start and src_len
6340     cbcCrypt = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
6341                                  OptoRuntime::cipherBlockChaining_aescrypt_Type(),
6342                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6343                                  src_start, dest_start, k_start, r_start, len);
6344   }
6345 
6346   // return cipher length (int)
6347   Node* retvalue = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(cbcCrypt, TypeFunc::Parms));
6348   set_result(retvalue);
6349   return true;
6350 }

6440 //------------------------------inline_counterMode_AESCrypt-----------------------
6441 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_counterMode_AESCrypt(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
6442   assert(UseAES, "need AES instruction support");
6443   if (!UseAESCTRIntrinsics) return false;
6444 
6445   address stubAddr = NULL;
6446   const char *stubName = NULL;
6447   if (id == vmIntrinsics::_counterMode_AESCrypt) {
6448     stubAddr = StubRoutines::counterMode_AESCrypt();
6449     stubName = "counterMode_AESCrypt";
6450   }
6451   if (stubAddr == NULL) return false;
6452 
6453   Node* counterMode_object = argument(0);
6454   Node* src = argument(1);
6455   Node* src_offset = argument(2);
6456   Node* len = argument(3);
6457   Node* dest = argument(4);
6458   Node* dest_offset = argument(5);
6459 
6460   // (1) src and dest are arrays.
6461   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
6462   const Type* dest_type = dest->Value(&_gvn);
6463   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
6464   const TypeAryPtr* top_dest = dest_type->isa_aryptr();
6465   assert(top_src != NULL && top_src->klass() != NULL &&
6466          top_dest != NULL && top_dest->klass() != NULL, "args are strange");
6467 
6468   // checks are the responsibility of the caller
6469   Node* src_start = src;
6470   Node* dest_start = dest;
6471   if (src_offset != NULL || dest_offset != NULL) {
6472     assert(src_offset != NULL && dest_offset != NULL, "");
6473     src_start = array_element_address(src, src_offset, T_BYTE);
6474     dest_start = array_element_address(dest, dest_offset, T_BYTE);
6475   }
6476 
6477   // if we are in this set of code, we "know" the embeddedCipher is an AESCrypt object
6478   // (because of the predicated logic executed earlier).
6479   // so we cast it here safely.
6480   // this requires a newer class file that has this array as littleEndian ints, otherwise we revert to java
6481   Node* embeddedCipherObj = load_field_from_object(counterMode_object, "embeddedCipher", "Lcom/sun/crypto/provider/SymmetricCipher;", /*is_exact*/ false);
6482   if (embeddedCipherObj == NULL) return false;
6483   // cast it to what we know it will be at runtime
6484   const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(counterMode_object)->isa_instptr();
6485   assert(tinst != NULL, "CTR obj is null");
6486   assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "CTR obj is not loaded");
6487   ciKlass* klass_AESCrypt = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass()->find_klass(ciSymbol::make("com/sun/crypto/provider/AESCrypt"));
6488   assert(klass_AESCrypt->is_loaded(), "predicate checks that this class is loaded");
6489   ciInstanceKlass* instklass_AESCrypt = klass_AESCrypt->as_instance_klass();
6490   const TypeKlassPtr* aklass = TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_AESCrypt);
6491   const TypeOopPtr* xtype = aklass->as_instance_type();
6492   Node* aescrypt_object = new CheckCastPPNode(control(), embeddedCipherObj, xtype);
6493   aescrypt_object = _gvn.transform(aescrypt_object);
6494   // we need to get the start of the aescrypt_object's expanded key array
6495   Node* k_start = get_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(aescrypt_object);
6496   if (k_start == NULL) return false;
6497   // similarly, get the start address of the r vector
6498   Node* obj_counter = load_field_from_object(counterMode_object, "counter", "[B", /*is_exact*/ false);
6499   if (obj_counter == NULL) return false;
6500   Node* cnt_start = array_element_address(obj_counter, intcon(0), T_BYTE);
6501 
6502   Node* saved_encCounter = load_field_from_object(counterMode_object, "encryptedCounter", "[B", /*is_exact*/ false);
6503   if (saved_encCounter == NULL) return false;
6504   Node* saved_encCounter_start = array_element_address(saved_encCounter, intcon(0), T_BYTE);
6505   Node* used = field_address_from_object(counterMode_object, "used", "I", /*is_exact*/ false);
6506 
6507   Node* ctrCrypt;
6508   if (Matcher::pass_original_key_for_aes()) {
6509     // no SPARC version for AES/CTR intrinsics now.
6510     return false;
6511   }
6512   // Call the stub, passing src_start, dest_start, k_start, r_start and src_len
6513   ctrCrypt = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
6514                                OptoRuntime::counterMode_aescrypt_Type(),
6515                                stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6516                                src_start, dest_start, k_start, cnt_start, len, saved_encCounter_start, used);
6517 
6518   // return cipher length (int)
6519   Node* retvalue = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(ctrCrypt, TypeFunc::Parms));
6520   set_result(retvalue);
6521   return true;
6522 }
6523 
6524 //------------------------------get_key_start_from_aescrypt_object-----------------------
6525 Node * LibraryCallKit::get_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(Node *aescrypt_object) {
6526 #if defined(PPC64) || defined(S390)
6527   // MixColumns for decryption can be reduced by preprocessing MixColumns with round keys.
6528   // Intel's extention is based on this optimization and AESCrypt generates round keys by preprocessing MixColumns.
6529   // However, ppc64 vncipher processes MixColumns and requires the same round keys with encryption.
6530   // The ppc64 stubs of encryption and decryption use the same round keys (sessionK[0]).
6531   Node* objSessionK = load_field_from_object(aescrypt_object, "sessionK", "[[I", /*is_exact*/ false);
6532   assert (objSessionK != NULL, "wrong version of com.sun.crypto.provider.AESCrypt");
6533   if (objSessionK == NULL) {
6534     return (Node *) NULL;
6535   }
6536   Node* objAESCryptKey = load_array_element(control(), objSessionK, intcon(0), TypeAryPtr::OOPS);
6537 #else
6538   Node* objAESCryptKey = load_field_from_object(aescrypt_object, "K", "[I", /*is_exact*/ false);
6539 #endif // PPC64
6540   assert (objAESCryptKey != NULL, "wrong version of com.sun.crypto.provider.AESCrypt");
6541   if (objAESCryptKey == NULL) return (Node *) NULL;
6542 
6543   // now have the array, need to get the start address of the K array
6544   Node* k_start = array_element_address(objAESCryptKey, intcon(0), T_INT);
6545   return k_start;
6546 }
6547 
6548 //------------------------------get_original_key_start_from_aescrypt_object-----------------------
6549 Node * LibraryCallKit::get_original_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(Node *aescrypt_object) {
6550   Node* objAESCryptKey = load_field_from_object(aescrypt_object, "lastKey", "[B", /*is_exact*/ false);
6551   assert (objAESCryptKey != NULL, "wrong version of com.sun.crypto.provider.AESCrypt");
6552   if (objAESCryptKey == NULL) return (Node *) NULL;
6553 
6554   // now have the array, need to get the start address of the lastKey array
6555   Node* original_k_start = array_element_address(objAESCryptKey, intcon(0), T_BYTE);
6556   return original_k_start;
6557 }
6558 
6559 //----------------------------inline_cipherBlockChaining_AESCrypt_predicate----------------------------
6560 // Return node representing slow path of predicate check.
6561 // the pseudo code we want to emulate with this predicate is:
6562 // for encryption:
6563 //    if (embeddedCipherObj instanceof AESCrypt) do_intrinsic, else do_javapath
6564 // for decryption:
6565 //    if ((embeddedCipherObj instanceof AESCrypt) && (cipher!=plain)) do_intrinsic, else do_javapath
6566 //    note cipher==plain is more conservative than the original java code but that's OK
6567 //
6568 Node* LibraryCallKit::inline_cipherBlockChaining_AESCrypt_predicate(bool decrypting) {
6569   // The receiver was checked for NULL already.
6570   Node* objCBC = argument(0);
6571 
6572   Node* src = argument(1);
6573   Node* dest = argument(4);
6574 
6575   // Load embeddedCipher field of CipherBlockChaining object.
6576   Node* embeddedCipherObj = load_field_from_object(objCBC, "embeddedCipher", "Lcom/sun/crypto/provider/SymmetricCipher;", /*is_exact*/ false);
6577 
6578   // get AESCrypt klass for instanceOf check
6579   // AESCrypt might not be loaded yet if some other SymmetricCipher got us to this compile point
6580   // will have same classloader as CipherBlockChaining object
6581   const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(objCBC)->isa_instptr();
6582   assert(tinst != NULL, "CBCobj is null");
6583   assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "CBCobj is not loaded");
6584 
6585   // we want to do an instanceof comparison against the AESCrypt class
6586   ciKlass* klass_AESCrypt = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass()->find_klass(ciSymbol::make("com/sun/crypto/provider/AESCrypt"));
6587   if (!klass_AESCrypt->is_loaded()) {
6588     // if AESCrypt is not even loaded, we never take the intrinsic fast path
6589     Node* ctrl = control();
6590     set_control(top()); // no regular fast path
6591     return ctrl;
6592   }
6593 
6594   src = must_be_not_null(src, true);
6595   dest = must_be_not_null(dest, true);
6596 
6597   // Resolve oops to stable for CmpP below.
6598   ciInstanceKlass* instklass_AESCrypt = klass_AESCrypt->as_instance_klass();
6599 
6600   Node* instof = gen_instanceof(embeddedCipherObj, makecon(TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_AESCrypt)));
6601   Node* cmp_instof  = _gvn.transform(new CmpINode(instof, intcon(1)));
6602   Node* bool_instof  = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp_instof, BoolTest::ne));
6603 
6604   Node* instof_false = generate_guard(bool_instof, NULL, PROB_MIN);
6605 
6606   // for encryption, we are done
6607   if (!decrypting)
6608     return instof_false;  // even if it is NULL
6609 
6610   // for decryption, we need to add a further check to avoid
6611   // taking the intrinsic path when cipher and plain are the same
6612   // see the original java code for why.
6613   RegionNode* region = new RegionNode(3);
6614   region->init_req(1, instof_false);
6615 
6616   Node* cmp_src_dest = _gvn.transform(new CmpPNode(src, dest));
6617   Node* bool_src_dest = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp_src_dest, BoolTest::eq));
6618   Node* src_dest_conjoint = generate_guard(bool_src_dest, NULL, PROB_MIN);
6619   region->init_req(2, src_dest_conjoint);
6620 
6621   record_for_igvn(region);
6622   return _gvn.transform(region);
6623 }
6624 
6625 //----------------------------inline_electronicCodeBook_AESCrypt_predicate----------------------------
6626 // Return node representing slow path of predicate check.
6627 // the pseudo code we want to emulate with this predicate is:
6628 // for encryption:
6629 //    if (embeddedCipherObj instanceof AESCrypt) do_intrinsic, else do_javapath
6630 // for decryption:
6631 //    if ((embeddedCipherObj instanceof AESCrypt) && (cipher!=plain)) do_intrinsic, else do_javapath
6632 //    note cipher==plain is more conservative than the original java code but that's OK
6633 //
6634 Node* LibraryCallKit::inline_electronicCodeBook_AESCrypt_predicate(bool decrypting) {
6635   // The receiver was checked for NULL already.
6636   Node* objECB = argument(0);
6637 
6638   // Load embeddedCipher field of ElectronicCodeBook object.
6639   Node* embeddedCipherObj = load_field_from_object(objECB, "embeddedCipher", "Lcom/sun/crypto/provider/SymmetricCipher;", /*is_exact*/ false);
6640 
6641   // get AESCrypt klass for instanceOf check
6642   // AESCrypt might not be loaded yet if some other SymmetricCipher got us to this compile point
6643   // will have same classloader as ElectronicCodeBook object
6644   const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(objECB)->isa_instptr();
6645   assert(tinst != NULL, "ECBobj is null");
6646   assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "ECBobj is not loaded");
6647 
6648   // we want to do an instanceof comparison against the AESCrypt class
6649   ciKlass* klass_AESCrypt = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass()->find_klass(ciSymbol::make("com/sun/crypto/provider/AESCrypt"));
6650   if (!klass_AESCrypt->is_loaded()) {
6651     // if AESCrypt is not even loaded, we never take the intrinsic fast path
6652     Node* ctrl = control();
6653     set_control(top()); // no regular fast path
6654     return ctrl;
6655   }
6656   ciInstanceKlass* instklass_AESCrypt = klass_AESCrypt->as_instance_klass();
6657 
6658   Node* instof = gen_instanceof(embeddedCipherObj, makecon(TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_AESCrypt)));
6659   Node* cmp_instof = _gvn.transform(new CmpINode(instof, intcon(1)));
6660   Node* bool_instof = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp_instof, BoolTest::ne));
6661 
6662   Node* instof_false = generate_guard(bool_instof, NULL, PROB_MIN);
6663 
6664   // for encryption, we are done
6665   if (!decrypting)
6666     return instof_false;  // even if it is NULL
6667 
6668   // for decryption, we need to add a further check to avoid
6669   // taking the intrinsic path when cipher and plain are the same
6670   // see the original java code for why.
6671   RegionNode* region = new RegionNode(3);
6672   region->init_req(1, instof_false);
6673   Node* src = argument(1);
6674   Node* dest = argument(4);
6675   Node* cmp_src_dest = _gvn.transform(new CmpPNode(src, dest));
6676   Node* bool_src_dest = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp_src_dest, BoolTest::eq));
6677   Node* src_dest_conjoint = generate_guard(bool_src_dest, NULL, PROB_MIN);
6678   region->init_req(2, src_dest_conjoint);
6679 
6680   record_for_igvn(region);
6681   return _gvn.transform(region);
6682 }

6726 //------------------------------inline_ghash_processBlocks
6727 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_ghash_processBlocks() {
6728   address stubAddr;
6729   const char *stubName;
6730   assert(UseGHASHIntrinsics, "need GHASH intrinsics support");
6731 
6732   stubAddr = StubRoutines::ghash_processBlocks();
6733   stubName = "ghash_processBlocks";
6734 
6735   Node* data           = argument(0);
6736   Node* offset         = argument(1);
6737   Node* len            = argument(2);
6738   Node* state          = argument(3);
6739   Node* subkeyH        = argument(4);
6740 
6741   state = must_be_not_null(state, true);
6742   subkeyH = must_be_not_null(subkeyH, true);
6743   data = must_be_not_null(data, true);
6744 
6745   Node* state_start  = array_element_address(state, intcon(0), T_LONG);
6746   assert(state_start, "state is NULL");
6747   Node* subkeyH_start  = array_element_address(subkeyH, intcon(0), T_LONG);
6748   assert(subkeyH_start, "subkeyH is NULL");
6749   Node* data_start  = array_element_address(data, offset, T_BYTE);
6750   assert(data_start, "data is NULL");
6751 
6752   Node* ghash = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
6753                                   OptoRuntime::ghash_processBlocks_Type(),
6754                                   stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6755                                   state_start, subkeyH_start, data_start, len);
6756   return true;
6757 }

6791 //------------------------------inline_sha_implCompress-----------------------
6792 //
6793 // Calculate SHA (i.e., SHA-1) for single-block byte[] array.
6794 // void com.sun.security.provider.SHA.implCompress(byte[] buf, int ofs)
6795 //
6796 // Calculate SHA2 (i.e., SHA-244 or SHA-256) for single-block byte[] array.
6797 // void com.sun.security.provider.SHA2.implCompress(byte[] buf, int ofs)
6798 //
6799 // Calculate SHA5 (i.e., SHA-384 or SHA-512) for single-block byte[] array.
6800 // void com.sun.security.provider.SHA5.implCompress(byte[] buf, int ofs)
6801 //
6802 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_sha_implCompress(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
6803   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 2, "sha_implCompress has 2 parameters");
6804 
6805   Node* sha_obj = argument(0);
6806   Node* src     = argument(1); // type oop
6807   Node* ofs     = argument(2); // type int
6808 
6809   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
6810   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
6811   if (top_src  == NULL || top_src->klass()  == NULL) {
6812     // failed array check
6813     return false;
6814   }
6815   // Figure out the size and type of the elements we will be copying.
6816   BasicType src_elem = src_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
6817   if (src_elem != T_BYTE) {
6818     return false;
6819   }
6820   // 'src_start' points to src array + offset
6821   src = must_be_not_null(src, true);
6822   Node* src_start = array_element_address(src, ofs, src_elem);
6823   Node* state = NULL;
6824   address stubAddr;
6825   const char *stubName;
6826 
6827   switch(id) {
6828   case vmIntrinsics::_sha_implCompress:
6829     assert(UseSHA1Intrinsics, "need SHA1 instruction support");
6830     state = get_state_from_sha_object(sha_obj);
6831     stubAddr = StubRoutines::sha1_implCompress();
6832     stubName = "sha1_implCompress";
6833     break;
6834   case vmIntrinsics::_sha2_implCompress:
6835     assert(UseSHA256Intrinsics, "need SHA256 instruction support");
6836     state = get_state_from_sha_object(sha_obj);
6837     stubAddr = StubRoutines::sha256_implCompress();
6838     stubName = "sha256_implCompress";
6839     break;
6840   case vmIntrinsics::_sha5_implCompress:
6841     assert(UseSHA512Intrinsics, "need SHA512 instruction support");
6842     state = get_state_from_sha5_object(sha_obj);
6843     stubAddr = StubRoutines::sha512_implCompress();
6844     stubName = "sha512_implCompress";
6845     break;
6846   default:
6847     fatal_unexpected_iid(id);
6848     return false;
6849   }
6850   if (state == NULL) return false;
6851 
6852   assert(stubAddr != NULL, "Stub is generated");
6853   if (stubAddr == NULL) return false;
6854 
6855   // Call the stub.
6856   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP, OptoRuntime::sha_implCompress_Type(),
6857                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6858                                  src_start, state);
6859 
6860   return true;
6861 }
6862 
6863 //------------------------------inline_digestBase_implCompressMB-----------------------
6864 //
6865 // Calculate SHA/SHA2/SHA5 for multi-block byte[] array.
6866 // int com.sun.security.provider.DigestBase.implCompressMultiBlock(byte[] b, int ofs, int limit)
6867 //
6868 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_digestBase_implCompressMB(int predicate) {
6869   assert(UseSHA1Intrinsics || UseSHA256Intrinsics || UseSHA512Intrinsics,
6870          "need SHA1/SHA256/SHA512 instruction support");
6871   assert((uint)predicate < 3, "sanity");
6872   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 3, "digestBase_implCompressMB has 3 parameters");
6873 
6874   Node* digestBase_obj = argument(0); // The receiver was checked for NULL already.
6875   Node* src            = argument(1); // byte[] array
6876   Node* ofs            = argument(2); // type int
6877   Node* limit          = argument(3); // type int
6878 
6879   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
6880   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
6881   if (top_src  == NULL || top_src->klass()  == NULL) {
6882     // failed array check
6883     return false;
6884   }
6885   // Figure out the size and type of the elements we will be copying.
6886   BasicType src_elem = src_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
6887   if (src_elem != T_BYTE) {
6888     return false;
6889   }
6890   // 'src_start' points to src array + offset
6891   src = must_be_not_null(src, false);
6892   Node* src_start = array_element_address(src, ofs, src_elem);
6893 
6894   const char* klass_SHA_name = NULL;
6895   const char* stub_name = NULL;
6896   address     stub_addr = NULL;
6897   bool        long_state = false;
6898 
6899   switch (predicate) {
6900   case 0:
6901     if (UseSHA1Intrinsics) {
6902       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA";
6903       stub_name = "sha1_implCompressMB";
6904       stub_addr = StubRoutines::sha1_implCompressMB();
6905     }
6906     break;
6907   case 1:
6908     if (UseSHA256Intrinsics) {
6909       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA2";
6910       stub_name = "sha256_implCompressMB";
6911       stub_addr = StubRoutines::sha256_implCompressMB();
6912     }
6913     break;
6914   case 2:
6915     if (UseSHA512Intrinsics) {
6916       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA5";
6917       stub_name = "sha512_implCompressMB";
6918       stub_addr = StubRoutines::sha512_implCompressMB();
6919       long_state = true;
6920     }
6921     break;
6922   default:
6923     fatal("unknown SHA intrinsic predicate: %d", predicate);
6924   }
6925   if (klass_SHA_name != NULL) {
6926     assert(stub_addr != NULL, "Stub is generated");
6927     if (stub_addr == NULL) return false;
6928 
6929     // get DigestBase klass to lookup for SHA klass
6930     const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(digestBase_obj)->isa_instptr();
6931     assert(tinst != NULL, "digestBase_obj is not instance???");
6932     assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "DigestBase is not loaded");
6933 
6934     ciKlass* klass_SHA = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass()->find_klass(ciSymbol::make(klass_SHA_name));
6935     assert(klass_SHA->is_loaded(), "predicate checks that this class is loaded");
6936     ciInstanceKlass* instklass_SHA = klass_SHA->as_instance_klass();
6937     return inline_sha_implCompressMB(digestBase_obj, instklass_SHA, long_state, stub_addr, stub_name, src_start, ofs, limit);
6938   }
6939   return false;
6940 }
6941 //------------------------------inline_sha_implCompressMB-----------------------
6942 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_sha_implCompressMB(Node* digestBase_obj, ciInstanceKlass* instklass_SHA,
6943                                                bool long_state, address stubAddr, const char *stubName,
6944                                                Node* src_start, Node* ofs, Node* limit) {
6945   const TypeKlassPtr* aklass = TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_SHA);
6946   const TypeOopPtr* xtype = aklass->as_instance_type();
6947   Node* sha_obj = new CheckCastPPNode(control(), digestBase_obj, xtype);
6948   sha_obj = _gvn.transform(sha_obj);
6949 
6950   Node* state;
6951   if (long_state) {
6952     state = get_state_from_sha5_object(sha_obj);
6953   } else {
6954     state = get_state_from_sha_object(sha_obj);
6955   }
6956   if (state == NULL) return false;
6957 
6958   // Call the stub.
6959   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
6960                                  OptoRuntime::digestBase_implCompressMB_Type(),
6961                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6962                                  src_start, state, ofs, limit);
6963   // return ofs (int)
6964   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(call, TypeFunc::Parms));
6965   set_result(result);
6966 
6967   return true;
6968 }
6969 
6970 //------------------------------get_state_from_sha_object-----------------------
6971 Node * LibraryCallKit::get_state_from_sha_object(Node *sha_object) {
6972   Node* sha_state = load_field_from_object(sha_object, "state", "[I", /*is_exact*/ false);
6973   assert (sha_state != NULL, "wrong version of sun.security.provider.SHA/SHA2");
6974   if (sha_state == NULL) return (Node *) NULL;
6975 
6976   // now have the array, need to get the start address of the state array
6977   Node* state = array_element_address(sha_state, intcon(0), T_INT);
6978   return state;
6979 }
6980 
6981 //------------------------------get_state_from_sha5_object-----------------------
6982 Node * LibraryCallKit::get_state_from_sha5_object(Node *sha_object) {
6983   Node* sha_state = load_field_from_object(sha_object, "state", "[J", /*is_exact*/ false);
6984   assert (sha_state != NULL, "wrong version of sun.security.provider.SHA5");
6985   if (sha_state == NULL) return (Node *) NULL;
6986 
6987   // now have the array, need to get the start address of the state array
6988   Node* state = array_element_address(sha_state, intcon(0), T_LONG);
6989   return state;
6990 }
6991 
6992 //----------------------------inline_digestBase_implCompressMB_predicate----------------------------
6993 // Return node representing slow path of predicate check.
6994 // the pseudo code we want to emulate with this predicate is:
6995 //    if (digestBaseObj instanceof SHA/SHA2/SHA5) do_intrinsic, else do_javapath
6996 //
6997 Node* LibraryCallKit::inline_digestBase_implCompressMB_predicate(int predicate) {
6998   assert(UseSHA1Intrinsics || UseSHA256Intrinsics || UseSHA512Intrinsics,
6999          "need SHA1/SHA256/SHA512 instruction support");
7000   assert((uint)predicate < 3, "sanity");
7001 
7002   // The receiver was checked for NULL already.
7003   Node* digestBaseObj = argument(0);
7004 
7005   // get DigestBase klass for instanceOf check
7006   const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(digestBaseObj)->isa_instptr();
7007   assert(tinst != NULL, "digestBaseObj is null");
7008   assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "DigestBase is not loaded");
7009 
7010   const char* klass_SHA_name = NULL;
7011   switch (predicate) {
7012   case 0:
7013     if (UseSHA1Intrinsics) {
7014       // we want to do an instanceof comparison against the SHA class
7015       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA";
7016     }
7017     break;
7018   case 1:
7019     if (UseSHA256Intrinsics) {
7020       // we want to do an instanceof comparison against the SHA2 class
7021       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA2";
7022     }
7023     break;
7024   case 2:
7025     if (UseSHA512Intrinsics) {
7026       // we want to do an instanceof comparison against the SHA5 class
7027       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA5";
7028     }
7029     break;
7030   default:
7031     fatal("unknown SHA intrinsic predicate: %d", predicate);
7032   }
7033 
7034   ciKlass* klass_SHA = NULL;
7035   if (klass_SHA_name != NULL) {
7036     klass_SHA = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass()->find_klass(ciSymbol::make(klass_SHA_name));
7037   }
7038   if ((klass_SHA == NULL) || !klass_SHA->is_loaded()) {
7039     // if none of SHA/SHA2/SHA5 is loaded, we never take the intrinsic fast path
7040     Node* ctrl = control();
7041     set_control(top()); // no intrinsic path
7042     return ctrl;
7043   }
7044   ciInstanceKlass* instklass_SHA = klass_SHA->as_instance_klass();
7045 
7046   Node* instofSHA = gen_instanceof(digestBaseObj, makecon(TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_SHA)));
7047   Node* cmp_instof = _gvn.transform(new CmpINode(instofSHA, intcon(1)));
7048   Node* bool_instof = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp_instof, BoolTest::ne));
7049   Node* instof_false = generate_guard(bool_instof, NULL, PROB_MIN);
7050 
7051   return instof_false;  // even if it is NULL
7052 }
7053 
7054 //-------------inline_fma-----------------------------------
7055 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_fma(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
7056   Node *a = NULL;
7057   Node *b = NULL;
7058   Node *c = NULL;
7059   Node* result = NULL;
7060   switch (id) {
7061   case vmIntrinsics::_fmaD:
7062     assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 6, "fma has 3 parameters of size 2 each.");
7063     // no receiver since it is static method
7064     a = round_double_node(argument(0));
7065     b = round_double_node(argument(2));
7066     c = round_double_node(argument(4));
7067     result = _gvn.transform(new FmaDNode(control(), a, b, c));
7068     break;
7069   case vmIntrinsics::_fmaF:
7070     assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 3, "fma has 3 parameters of size 1 each.");
7071     a = argument(0);
7072     b = argument(1);
7073     c = argument(2);
7074     result = _gvn.transform(new FmaFNode(control(), a, b, c));
7075     break;
7076   default:
7077     fatal_unexpected_iid(id);  break;
7078   }
7079   set_result(result);
7080   return true;
7081 }
7082 
7083 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_character_compare(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
7084   // argument(0) is receiver
7085   Node* codePoint = argument(1);
7086   Node* n = NULL;
7087 
7088   switch (id) {
7089     case vmIntrinsics::_isDigit :
7090       n = new DigitNode(control(), codePoint);
7091       break;
7092     case vmIntrinsics::_isLowerCase :
7093       n = new LowerCaseNode(control(), codePoint);
7094       break;
7095     case vmIntrinsics::_isUpperCase :
7096       n = new UpperCaseNode(control(), codePoint);
7097       break;
7098     case vmIntrinsics::_isWhitespace :
7099       n = new WhitespaceNode(control(), codePoint);
7100       break;
7101     default:
7102       fatal_unexpected_iid(id);
7103   }
7104 
7105   set_result(_gvn.transform(n));
7106   return true;
7107 }
7108 
7109 //------------------------------inline_fp_min_max------------------------------
7110 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_fp_min_max(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
7111 /* DISABLED BECAUSE METHOD DATA ISN'T COLLECTED PER CALL-SITE, SEE JDK-8015416.
7112 
7113   // The intrinsic should be used only when the API branches aren't predictable,
7114   // the last one performing the most important comparison. The following heuristic
7115   // uses the branch statistics to eventually bail out if necessary.
7116 
7117   ciMethodData *md = callee()->method_data();
7118 
7119   if ( md != NULL && md->is_mature() && md->invocation_count() > 0 ) {
7120     ciCallProfile cp = caller()->call_profile_at_bci(bci());
7121 
7122     if ( ((double)cp.count()) / ((double)md->invocation_count()) < 0.8 ) {
7123       // Bail out if the call-site didn't contribute enough to the statistics.
7124       return false;
7125     }
7126 
7127     uint taken = 0, not_taken = 0;
7128 
7129     for (ciProfileData *p = md->first_data(); md->is_valid(p); p = md->next_data(p)) {
7130       if (p->is_BranchData()) {
7131         taken = ((ciBranchData*)p)->taken();
7132         not_taken = ((ciBranchData*)p)->not_taken();
7133       }
7134     }
7135 
7136     double balance = (((double)taken) - ((double)not_taken)) / ((double)md->invocation_count());
7137     balance = balance < 0 ? -balance : balance;
7138     if ( balance > 0.2 ) {
7139       // Bail out if the most important branch is predictable enough.
7140       return false;
7141     }
7142   }
7143 */
7144 
7145   Node *a = NULL;
7146   Node *b = NULL;
7147   Node *n = NULL;
7148   switch (id) {
7149   case vmIntrinsics::_maxF:
7150   case vmIntrinsics::_minF:
7151     assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 2, "minF/maxF has 2 parameters of size 1 each.");
7152     a = argument(0);
7153     b = argument(1);
7154     break;
7155   case vmIntrinsics::_maxD:
7156   case vmIntrinsics::_minD:
7157     assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 4, "minD/maxD has 2 parameters of size 2 each.");
7158     a = round_double_node(argument(0));
7159     b = round_double_node(argument(2));
7160     break;
7161   default:
7162     fatal_unexpected_iid(id);
7163     break;
7164   }
7165   switch (id) {
7166   case vmIntrinsics::_maxF:  n = new MaxFNode(a, b);  break;
7167   case vmIntrinsics::_minF:  n = new MinFNode(a, b);  break;
7168   case vmIntrinsics::_maxD:  n = new MaxDNode(a, b);  break;
7169   case vmIntrinsics::_minD:  n = new MinDNode(a, b);  break;
7170   default:  fatal_unexpected_iid(id);  break;
7171   }
7172   set_result(_gvn.transform(n));
7173   return true;
7174 }
7175 
7176 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_profileBoolean() {
7177   Node* counts = argument(1);
7178   const TypeAryPtr* ary = NULL;
7179   ciArray* aobj = NULL;
7180   if (counts->is_Con()
7181       && (ary = counts->bottom_type()->isa_aryptr()) != NULL
7182       && (aobj = ary->const_oop()->as_array()) != NULL
7183       && (aobj->length() == 2)) {
7184     // Profile is int[2] where [0] and [1] correspond to false and true value occurrences respectively.
7185     jint false_cnt = aobj->element_value(0).as_int();
7186     jint  true_cnt = aobj->element_value(1).as_int();
7187 
7188     if (C->log() != NULL) {
7189       C->log()->elem("observe source='profileBoolean' false='%d' true='%d'",
7190                      false_cnt, true_cnt);
7191     }
7192 
7193     if (false_cnt + true_cnt == 0) {
7194       // According to profile, never executed.
7195       uncommon_trap_exact(Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic,
7196                           Deoptimization::Action_reinterpret);
7197       return true;
7198     }
7199 
7200     // result is a boolean (0 or 1) and its profile (false_cnt & true_cnt)
7201     // is a number of each value occurrences.
7202     Node* result = argument(0);
7203     if (false_cnt == 0 || true_cnt == 0) {
7204       // According to profile, one value has been never seen.
7205       int expected_val = (false_cnt == 0) ? 1 : 0;
7206 
7207       Node* cmp  = _gvn.transform(new CmpINode(result, intcon(expected_val)));
7208       Node* test = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp, BoolTest::eq));
7209 
7210       IfNode* check = create_and_map_if(control(), test, PROB_ALWAYS, COUNT_UNKNOWN);
7211       Node* fast_path = _gvn.transform(new IfTrueNode(check));
7212       Node* slow_path = _gvn.transform(new IfFalseNode(check));
7213 
7214       { // Slow path: uncommon trap for never seen value and then reexecute
7215         // MethodHandleImpl::profileBoolean() to bump the count, so JIT knows
7216         // the value has been seen at least once.
7217         PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
7218         PreserveReexecuteState preexecs(this);
7219         jvms()->set_should_reexecute(true);
7220 
7221         set_control(slow_path);
7222         set_i_o(i_o());
7223 
7224         uncommon_trap_exact(Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic,
7225                             Deoptimization::Action_reinterpret);
7226       }
7227       // The guard for never seen value enables sharpening of the result and
7228       // returning a constant. It allows to eliminate branches on the same value
7229       // later on.
7230       set_control(fast_path);
7231       result = intcon(expected_val);
7232     }
7233     // Stop profiling.
7234     // MethodHandleImpl::profileBoolean() has profiling logic in its bytecode.
7235     // By replacing method body with profile data (represented as ProfileBooleanNode
7236     // on IR level) we effectively disable profiling.
7237     // It enables full speed execution once optimized code is generated.
7238     Node* profile = _gvn.transform(new ProfileBooleanNode(result, false_cnt, true_cnt));
7239     C->record_for_igvn(profile);
7240     set_result(profile);
7241     return true;
7242   } else {
7243     // Continue profiling.
7244     // Profile data isn't available at the moment. So, execute method's bytecode version.
7245     // Usually, when GWT LambdaForms are profiled it means that a stand-alone nmethod
7246     // is compiled and counters aren't available since corresponding MethodHandle
7247     // isn't a compile-time constant.
7248     return false;
7249   }
7250 }
7251 
7252 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_isCompileConstant() {
7253   Node* n = argument(0);
7254   set_result(n->is_Con() ? intcon(1) : intcon(0));
7255   return true;
7256 }
